Conclusion: 该工作表明3DGS中常用的α-blending特征优化不适合直接用于精确匹配；通过构建无偏地标特征并结合可靠采样与几何验证，ULF-Loc在定位精度和计算效率上均取得改进。

Abstract: Visual localization is a core technology for augmented reality and autonomous navigation. Recent methods combine the efficient rendering of 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) with feature-based localization. These methods rely on direct matching between 2D query features and the 3D Gaussian feature field, but this often results in mismatches due to an inherent bias in the learned Gaussian feature. We theoretically analyze the feature learning process in 3DGS, revealing that the widely adopted $α$-blending optimization inherently introduces bias into 3D point features. This bias stems from the entanglement between individual Gaussians and their neighboring Gaussians, making the learned features unsuitable for precise matching tasks. Motivated by these findings, we propose ULF-Loc, an unbiased landmark feature framework that replaces biased feature optimization with geometry-weighted feature fusion. We further introduce keypoint-consensus landmark sampling to select reliable Gaussians and local geometric consistency verification to reject mismatches caused by rendering artifacts. On the Cambridge Landmarks dataset, ULF-Loc reduces the mean median translation error by 17\% compared to the state-of-the-art, while achieving superior efficiency with only 1/10 the training time and 1/6 the GPU memory of STDLoc.

In this paper, we propose FairEnc, a fair pretraining method for vision-language models (VLMs) that enables simultaneous debiasing across multiple sensitive attributes. FairEnc jointly mitigates biases in both textual and visual modalities with respect to multiple sensitive attributes, including race, gender, ethnicity, and language. Specifically, for the textual encoder, we leverage a large language model to generate synthetic clinical descriptions with varied sensitive attributes while preserving disease semantics, and employ a contrastive alignment objective to encourage demographic-invariant representations. For the visual encoder, we propose a dual-level fairness strategy that combines mutual information regularization to reduce statistical dependence between learned features and demographic groups, with multi-discriminator adversarial debiasing. Comprehensive experiments on the publicly available Harvard-FairVLMed dataset demonstrate that FairEnc effectively reduces demographic disparity as measured by DPD and DEOdds while achieving strong diagnostic performance under both zero-shot and linear probing evaluations. Motivation: 单通道热图像缺乏颜色信息、纹理信息弱，同类目标外观相似；同时视角变化会导致特征显著变化，使现有方法在车辆与海上船舶等细粒度识别任务中表现不佳。

Method: 方法利用RGB预训练的ViT特征提取器，并将其适配到热成像域；核心包括构建视角条件化的特征向量，以及在独立特征空间中进行区域特定的特征比较，以更好地利用形状和局部区域差异。

Result: 在RGBNT100红外车辆数据集和作者自采的热成像海事数据集上进行测试，mAP分别较现有最优方法提升19.7%和12.8%。

Conclusion: 该方法有效缓解了热成像目标识别中颜色缺失、纹理弱化和视角变化带来的困难，显著提升了单通道热图像下的目标识别性能；作者还计划公开首个海事船舶热成像识别数据集。

Abstract: Identification of less-articulated objects using single-channel images, such as thermal images, is important in many applications, such as surveillance. However, in this domain, existing methods show poor performance due to high similarity among objects of the same category in the absence of color information (overlooking shape information) and de-emphasized texture information. Furthermore, variability in viewpoint adds more complexity as the features vary from side to side. We address these issues by constructing viewpoint-conditioned feature vectors and area-specific feature comparisons in separate feature spaces. These interventions enable leveraging the advancements of existing RGB-pre-trained ViT feature extractors while effectively adapting them to address the challenges specific to the thermal domain. We test our system with RGBNT100 (IR) vehicle dataset and a thermal maritime dataset acquired by us. Our results surpass the state-of-the-art methods by 19.7% and 12.8% for the above datasets in mAP scores, respectively. We also plan to make our thermal dataset available, the first of its kind for maritime vessel identification.

</details>


### [51] [DART: A Vision-Language Foundation Model for Comprehensive Rope Condition Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04943)
*Anju Rani,Daniel Ortiz-Arroyo,Petar Durdevic*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DART是面向合成纤维绳索巡检的视觉-语言基础模型，可从单张图像统一输出损伤分类、严重度估计、异常提示和维护相关信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统绳索状态监测方法通常局限于分类，难以满足实际巡检中对连续严重度、维护建议、异常检测、劣化趋势和自动报告等综合信息的需求。

Method: 提出DART，将ViT-H/14与Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct通过严重度条件跨模态融合模块结合，并扩展JEPA到跨模态场景；引入HD-MASK、按类别可学习严重度门控和CDD损失，以增强损伤区域建模、类别相关语言对齐和损伤表征解耦。

Result: 在4270张、14类细粒度绳索损伤图像上训练后，冻结骨干即可支持下游任务：分类准确率93.22%、macro-F1为91.04%，严重度回归Spearman rho为0.94，within-1-ordinal准确率99.6%，20-shot少样本macro-F1为89.2%。

Abstract: The condition monitoring (CM) of synthetic fibre ropes (SFRs) used in offshore, maritime, and industrial settings demands more than a classifier: inspectors need continuous severity estimates, maintenance recommendations, anomaly flags, deterioration timelines, and automated reports, all from a single inspection image. We present DART (Damage Assessment via Rope Transformer), a vision-language foundation model that addresses the full rope inspection workflow through a unified multi-task architecture. DART extends the Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) to the cross-modal domain by coupling a Vision Transformer (ViT-H/14) with Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct via a Severity-Conditioned Cross-Modal Fusion (SC-CMF) module. Three architectural innovations drive the model's versatility: (1) HD-MASK, a saliency-guided masking strategy that focuses self-supervised reconstruction on damage-dense patches; (2) per-class learnable severity gates that adaptively weight language grounding by damage category; and (3) a Contrastive Damage Disentanglement (CDD) loss that shapes the embedding space to simultaneously encode damage type, severity ordering, and cross-modal semantics. Trained once on 4,270 images spanning 14 fine-grained rope damage classes, the frozen DART backbone supports downstream tasks without any task-specific fine-tuning: damage classification (93.22 % accuracy, 91.04 % macro-F1, +38.5 pp over a vision-only baseline), continuous severity regression (Spearman rho = 0.94, within-1-ordinal accuracy 99.6 %), few-shot recognition (89.2 % macro-F1 at 20 shots). These results demonstrate that DART functions as a general-purpose CM backbone that goes well beyond classification, providing actionable inspection intelligence from a single shared representation.

### [53] [Gaze4HRI: Zero-shot Benchmarking Gaze Estimation Neural-Networks for Human-Robot Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04770)
*Berk Sezer,Ali Görkem Küçük,Erol Şahin,Sinan Kalkan*

Main category: cs.CV

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本外观式3D凝视估计评测往往忽略HRI中的关键真实条件，如相机视角变化、视频中目标移动等；跨数据集评估还存在训练集复杂而测试集过小、变化不足的“复杂度差距”，难以真实衡量模型鲁棒性。

Method: 构建大规模数据集 Gaze4HRI，包含50余名受试者、3000余段视频、60万余帧，并围绕光照、头部与凝视方向冲突、相机运动、凝视目标运动等HRI变量，对多种最先进零样本3D凝视估计方法进行基准评测。

Result: 所有被评估方法至少在一种条件下失效，其中陡峭向下凝视是普遍失败点。PureGaze 在 ETH-X-Gaze 数据集上训练时，除该普遍失效条件外，在其他条件下表现出相对稳定的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，相比复杂时空建模和Transformer架构，训练数据的广泛多样性是零样本鲁棒性的主要驱动力；同时，PureGaze 的自对抗损失等凝视特征净化机制可进一步提升鲁棒性。Gaze4HRI 为HRI中的凝视估计提供了更严格的评测基准和实践指导。

Abstract: While zero-shot appearance-based 3D gaze estimation offers significant cost-efficiency by directly mapping RGB images to gaze vectors, its reliability in Human-Robot Interaction (HRI) settings remains uncertain. Existing benchmarks frequently overlook fundamental HRI conditions, such as dynamic camera viewpoints and moving targets in video. Furthermore, current cross-dataset evaluations often suffer from a complexity gap, where methods trained on diverse datasets are tested on significantly smaller and less varied sets, failing to assess true robustness. To bridge these gaps, we introduce Gaze4HRI, a large-scale dataset (50+ subjects, 3,000+ videos, 600,000+ frames) designed to evaluate state-of-the-art performance against critical HRI variables: illumination, head-gaze conflict, as well as the motion of camera and gaze target in video. Our benchmark reveals that all evaluated methods fail in at least one condition, identifying steeply-downward gaze as a universal failure point. Notably, PureGaze trained on the ETH-X-Gaze dataset uniquely maintains resilience across all other conditions. These results challenge the recent focus in the literature on complex spatial-temporal modeling and Transformer-based architectures. Instead, our findings suggest that extensive data diversity, as exemplified by the ETH-X-Gaze dataset, serves as the primary driver of zero-shot robustness in unconstrained environments, while resilience-enhancing frameworks, such as PureGaze's self-adversarial loss for gaze feature purification, provide a substantial further improvement. Ultimately, this study establishes a rigorous benchmark that provides practical guidelines for practitioners as well as reshaping future research. The dataset and codes are available at https://gazeforhri.github.io.

### [54] [Local Intrinsic Dimension Unveils Hallucinations in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05026)
*Bartlomiej Sobieski,Matthew Tivnan,Dawid Płudowski,Michał Jan Włodarczyk,Pengfei Jin,Przemyslaw Biecek,Quanzheng Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文将扩散模型的结构性幻觉解释为模型诱导流形上的不稳定性，并提出通过降低局部内在维度来抑制幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型会生成符合训练数据统计特征但违反结构规则的样本，例如解剖结构不一致。已有解释如模式插值只能部分说明原因，因此需要新的机制性视角和更有效的纠正方法。

Method: 作者先构建基于流形不稳定性的幻觉过滤器，并与时间一致性类过滤方法比较；随后追踪不稳定性的来源，发现局部内在维度（LID）是主要驱动因素；据此提出 Intrinsic Quenching（IQ），通过直接压低/收缩 LID 来缓解结构性幻觉。

Result: 基于不稳定性的过滤器达到或超过近期提出的时间过滤器；IQ 在多种基准上持续优于标准幻觉减少方法，并在医学影像下游任务中显示出提升解剖一致性的潜力。

Conclusion: 结构性幻觉可被理解为模型诱导流形上的局部不稳定现象，而降低局部内在维度是一种有效的直接干预手段，可增强扩散模型生成结果的结构一致性。

Abstract: Diffusion models are prone to generating structural hallucinations - samples that match the statistical properties of the training data yet defy underlying structural rules, resulting in anomalies like hands with more than five fingers. Recent research studied this failure mode from several viewpoints, offering partial explanations to their occurrence, such as mode interpolation. In this work, we propose a complementary perspective that treats hallucinations as instabilities on the model-induced manifold. We begin by showing that a hallucination filter based on such instabilities matches or exceeds the performance of the recently proposed temporal one. By tracing the source of these instabilities, we identify local intrinsic dimension (LID) as their primary driver and propose Intrinsic Quenching (IQ), a direct corrective mechanism that deflates it to alleviate hallucinations. IQ consistently outperforms standard hallucination reduction baselines across a wide array of benchmarks and offers a highly promising solution for enforcing anatomical consistency in downstream medical imaging tasks.

### [56] [Direct Product Flow Matching: Decoupling Radial and Angular Dynamics for Few-Shot Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05054)
*Hongxu Chen,Yanghao Wang,Bowei Zhu,Hongxiang Li,Zhen Wang,Ziqi Jiang,Lin Li,Rui Liu,Long Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出现有流匹配方法在预训练跨模态特征的几何先验上存在不兼容问题，提出基于翘曲积/直积流匹配的几何框架，以解耦径向与角向动态并提升少样本适配性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有流匹配方法将视觉-语言模型的跨模态对齐建模为连续多步流，但由于通常在归一化特征空间中处理，忽略了特征的径向信息，并引入径向-角向耦合，导致角向运动速度不均、训练困难、截断误差增加，以及无法恢复数据集特定信息。

Method: 作者从极分解视角分析跨模态特征，将其划分为径向与角向子流形；提出翘曲积流匹配（WP-FM）这一统一黎曼几何框架，并在常数翘曲度量下推导出直积流匹配（DP-FM）。DP-FM在直积/柱面流形上实现径向演化与角向测地传输的解耦，同时引入基于预训练视觉-语言模型隐藏状态的无分类器指导，以补充数据集上下文信息。

Result: 在11个基准数据集上的实验表明，DP-FM在多步少样本适配任务中达到新的最先进性能，优于已有流匹配适配方法。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，显式建模跨模态特征的径向与角向几何结构有助于缓解现有FM方法的动态失真与信息丢失问题；DP-FM通过解耦几何流与上下文条件指导，实现了更稳定且更有效的视觉-语言模型少样本适配。

Abstract: Recent flow matching (FM) methods improve the few-shot adaptation of vision-language models, by modeling cross-modal alignment as a continuous multi-step flow. In this paper, we argue that existing FM methods are inherently constrained by incompatible geometric priors on pre-trained cross-modal features, resulting in suboptimal adaptation performance. We first analyze these methods from a polar decomposition perspective (i.e., radial and angular sub-manifolds). Under this new geometric view, we identify three overlooked limitations in them: 1) Angular dynamics distortion: The radial-angular coupling induces non-uniform speed on the angular sub-manifold, leading to regression training difficulty and extra truncation errors. 2) Radial dynamics neglect: Feature normalization discards modality confidence, failing to distinguish out-of-distribution and in-distribution data, and abandoning crucial radial dynamics. 3) Context-agnostic unconditional flow: Dataset-specific information loss during pre-trained cross-modal feature extraction remains unrecovered. To resolve these issues, we propose warped product flow matching (WP-FM), a unified Riemannian framework that reformulates alignment on a warped product manifold. Within this framework, we derive direct product flow matching (DP-FM) by introducing a constant-warping metric, which yields a decoupled cylindrical manifold (i.e., direct product manifold). DP-FM enables independent radial evolution and constant-speed angular geodesic transport, effectively eliminating angular dynamics distortion while preserving radial consistency. Meanwhile, we incorporate classifier-free guidance by conditioning the flow on the pre-trained VLMs' hidden states to inject missing dataset-specific information. Extensive results across 11 benchmarks have demonstrated that DP-FM achieves a new state-of-the-art for multi-step few-shot adaptation.

</details>


### [57] [QuadBox: Accelerating 3D Gaussian Splatting with Geometry-Aware Boxes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04844)
*Xinze Li,Bohan Yang,Pengxu Chen,Yiyuan Wang,Hongcheng Luo,Wentao Cheng,Weifeng Su*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: QuadBox通过用四个轴对齐包围盒紧密覆盖投影高斯，并配合单遍瓦片遍历算法QPass，加速3D Gaussian Splatting的光栅化渲染，实验实现1.85倍提速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在实时新视角合成中表现突出，但其光栅化流程需要高效且精确地计算投影高斯与屏幕瓦片的相交关系。传统方法可能包含大量无关瓦片，导致冗余相交检测和渲染开销。

Method: 论文提出QuadBox，用四个离散的轴对齐包围盒对投影后的椭圆高斯进行更紧密封装。首先推导几何感知的拉伸因子，使QuadBox与瓦片网格对齐并覆盖椭圆投影，同时尽量排除无关瓦片；其次提出QPass单遍瓦片遍历算法，利用QuadBox的离散结构，将瓦片相交判断简化为区间测试。

Result: 在公开数据集上的实验表明，该方法可将3DGS渲染速度提升至原来的1.85倍，说明其能显著降低光栅化阶段的瓦片遍历与相交检测开销。

Conclusion: QuadBox针对3DGS光栅化中的高斯-瓦片相交瓶颈，提供了一种兼顾紧致性、离散对齐和计算效率的加速方案，可有效提升实时渲染性能。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has emerged as an advanced technique for real-time novel view synthesis by representing scene geometry and appearance using differentiable Gaussian primitives. However, efficiently computing precise Gaussian-tile intersections remains a critical task in the rasterization pipeline. To this end, we propose QuadBox, a method that leverages four axis-aligned bounding boxes to tightly encapsulate projected Gaussians in a discrete manner. First, we derive a geometry-aware stretching factor that enables the construction of a tile-aligned QuadBox, which covers the elliptical projection and largely excludes irrelevant tiles. Second, we introduce QPass, a single-pass tile traversal algorithm that exhaustively exploits the discrete nature of QuadBox, ensuring that the tile intersection check is performed with simple interval tests. Experiments on public datasets show that our method accelerates the rendering speed of 3DGS by 1.85$\times$. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/Powertony102/QuadBox}{https://github.com/Powertony102/QuadBox}.

</details>


### [58] [VTAgent: Agentic Keyframe Anchoring for Evidence-Aware Video TextVQA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04870)
*Haibin He,Maoyuan Ye,Jing Zhang,Juhua Liu,Bo Du*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文指出现有 Video-LLM 在 Video TextVQA 上的主要瓶颈不是推理能力，而是无法准确定位与问题相关的关键帧；为此提出问题引导的智能体框架，先显式锚定关键帧再回答问题，并在训练自由、SFT 和 RL 设置下取得显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Video TextVQA 需要模型基于视频中的视觉文本进行问答。尽管近期 Video-LLM 具备较强的视频多模态理解能力，但在现有 Video TextVQA 基准上的表现仍有限。作者希望分析性能差距来源，并找到提升模型能力的关键方向。

Method: 作者首先进行逐帧问答的上界分析：若任一帧能给出正确答案，则该样本计为正确。该分析显示逐帧上界显著优于直接视频推理。基于此，作者提出问题引导的 agent 框架，在回答前显式定位并锚定与问题相关的关键帧。该方法可在无需训练的设置下运行，并可进一步结合监督微调和强化学习优化。

Result: 逐帧上界分析明显超过直接视频推理，揭示模型存在较大的证据定位差距。提出的方法在训练自由设置下稳定优于直接视频推理；结合 SFT 和 RL 后，在多个基准上平均准确率提升 +12.12，ANLS 提升 +11.15，并达到新的 state-of-the-art。

Conclusion: 论文认为 Video TextVQA 的核心挑战在于关键证据定位，尤其是与问题相关的关键帧锚定，而非单纯的推理能力不足。显式关键帧锚定是提升 Video TextVQA 性能的重要方向。

Abstract: Video text-based visual question answering (Video TextVQA) aims to answer questions by reasoning over visual textual content appearing in videos. Despite the strong multimodal video understanding capabilities of recent Video-LLMs, their performance on existing Video TextVQA benchmarks remains limited. To better understand this gap, we conduct an upper-bound analysis through frame-wise question answering, counting a sample as correct if any frame yields the right answer, which significantly outperforms direct video-based inference and reveals a substantial performance gap. The results suggest that the primary bottleneck lies in the localization of key question-relevant evidence, rather than in reasoning capacity itself. Building on this insight, we propose a question-guided agent framework that explicitly anchors the relevant keyframes before answering. The approach operates effectively in a training-free setting and consistently surpasses direct video inference. With additional supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL), it achieves an average improvement of +12.12 in accuracy and +11.15 in ANLS across benchmarks, establishing new state-of-the-art results. Our study underscores the critical role of explicit keyframe anchoring for advancing Video TextVQA. The code will be publicly released.

The evaluation protocol includes three tracks: RGB Re-ID, Depth Re-ID, and RGB$\leftrightarrow$Depth cross-modal retrieval. Submissions are ranked using mAP and CMC-1 under a unified server-side evaluation. The final results show a clear difficulty ordering (RGB $>$ Depth $>$ Cross-Modal), highlighting both the challenge of modality-constrained retrieval and the feasibility of strong performance with modality-invariant learning. By releasing the dataset at https://zenodo.org/records/17909410, the evaluation scripts at https://github.com/RaphaelDel/ICPR-TVRID, and the accompanying documentation, TVRID establishes a reproducible benchmark for top-view, depth-based, and cross-modal person re-id.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医学图像深度学习分类通常依赖大量标注数据或ImageNet迁移学习；常见自监督方法如MAE采用随机遮挡，可能破坏细粒度诊断特征，不利于医学图像中关键病灶信息的学习。

Method: 作者用混沌变换扰动输入图像，而非随机mask，并训练自编码器重建原图，使编码器学习“逆转混沌”所需的鲁棒领域特异性表征；随后设计注意力融合机制，将CDAE预训练编码器特征与标准编码器特征结合，用于最终分类。

Result: 在ISIC 2018皮肤病灶数据集上达到Accuracy 0.9221、F1-macro 0.8530；在APTOS 2019糖尿病视网膜病变数据集上达到Accuracy 0.8644、F1-macro 0.7433，显示出较强性能。

Conclusion: CDAE通过避免随机遮挡对诊断细节的破坏，能够学习更适合医学图像的自监督表征；与标准编码器的注意力融合进一步提升了分类效果，说明领域特异性与通用表征互补。

Abstract: Deep learning models for medical image classification usually achieve promising results but typically rely on large, annotated datasets or standard transfer learning from ImageNet. Self-Supervised Learning (SSL) has emerged as a powerful alternative, yet common methods like masked autoencoders (MAEs) may inadvertently destroy fine-grained diagnostic features by using random masking. In this paper, we propose a novel SSL pre-training strategy, the Chaotic Denoising Autoencoder (CDAE). Instead of masking, we apply a chaotic transformation to the input image, tasking an autoencoder to reconstruct the original. We hypothesize this forces the encoder to learn robust, domain-specific features by "inverting the chaos". Furthermore, we propose an attentive fusion mechanism that combines features from our CDAE-trained encoder with a standard encoder, leveraging the strengths of both general and domain-specific representations. Our method is evaluated on two public medical datasets: ISIC 2018 (skin lesions) and APTOS 2019 (diabetic retinopathy). The proposed model achieves high performance, with an accuracy of 0.9221 and an F1-macro of 0.8530 on ISIC 2018, and an accuracy of 0.8644 and F1-macro of 0.7433 on APTOS 2019, demonstrating the efficacy of our approach.

Leveraging 3,820 wildfire events from 2017-2023, we conduct spatial and temporal generalization tests across diverse biomes. We systematically compare full fine-tuning, decoder-only fine-tuning, and Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) for adapting each model. Across all experiments, LoRA provides the strongest cross-domain generalization while updating less than 1% of parameters, demonstrating a favorable trade-off between accuracy and efficiency. Prithvi-v2 with LoRA achieves the highest overall accuracy and the largest improvement compared to full fine-tuning. These findings indicate that geospatial foundation models, when adapted using lightweight parameter-efficient methods such as LoRA, offer a robust and scalable solution for large-scale burned-area mapping. ### [64] [Taming Outlier Tokens in Diffusion Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05206)
*Xiaoyu Wu,Yifei Wang,Tsu-Jui Fu,Liang-Chieh Chen,Zhe Gan,Chen Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究扩散 Transformer（DiT）图像生成中的异常 token 现象，提出 Dual-Stage Registers（DSR）在编码器与去噪器两阶段控制异常 token，从而减少伪影并提升生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究发现视觉 Transformer 会产生少量高范数 token，它们吸引过多注意力但局部语义信息有限；然而这类异常 token 在生成模型，尤其是 RAE-DiT 管线中的作用尚未被充分理解。

Method: 作者分析 RAE-DiT 中编码器与 DiT 去噪器的异常 token 分布与影响，发现简单屏蔽高范数 token 无法改善效果；据此提出 DSR：在编码器侧使用训练好的 registers 或测试时递归 registers，在去噪器侧引入 diffusion registers，以干预并吸收异常 token 影响。

Result: 在 ImageNet 与大规模文本到图像生成任务中，DSR 能稳定减少异常 token 引发的生成伪影，并提升整体生成质量。

Conclusion: 异常 token 控制是构建更强 DiT 生成模型的重要因素；问题不仅是极端高范数值本身，更与局部 patch 语义受损有关，register-based 双阶段干预是一种有效解决方案。

Abstract: We study outlier tokens in Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) for image generation. Prior work has shown that Vision Transformers (ViTs) can produce a small number of high-norm tokens that attract disproportionate attention while carrying limited local information, but their role in generative models remains underexplored. We show that this phenomenon appears in both the encoder and denoiser of modern Representation Autoencoder (RAE)-DiT pipelines: pretrained ViT encoders can produce outlier representations, and DiTs themselves can develop internal outlier tokens, especially in intermediate layers. Moreover, simply masking high-norm tokens does not improve performance, indicating that the problem is not only caused by a few extreme values, but is more closely related to corrupted local patch semantics. To address this issue, we introduce Dual-Stage Registers (DSR), a register-based intervention for both components: trained registers when available, recursive test-time registers otherwise, and diffusion registers for the denoiser. Across ImageNet and large-scale text-to-image generation, these interventions consistently reduce outlier artifacts and improve generation quality. Our results highlight outlier-token control as an important ingredient in building stronger DiTs.

</details>

*Gasser Elazab,Frank Neuhaus,Tilman Koß,Malte Splietker,Aditya Date,Michael Unterreiner,Maximilian Jansen,Olaf Hellwich*

Abstract: Autonomous driving must operate across diverse surfaces to enable safe mobility. However, most driving datasets are captured on well-paved flat roads. Moreover, recent driving datasets primarily provide sparse LiDAR ground truth for images, which is insufficient for assessing fine-grained geometry in depth estimation and completion. To address these gaps, we introduce CARD, a multi-modal driving dataset that delivers quasi-dense 3D ground truth across continuous sequences rich in speed bumps, potholes, irregular surfaces and off-road segments. Our sensor suite includes synchronized global-shutter stereo cameras, front and rear LiDARs, 6-DoF poses from LiDAR-inertial odometry, per-wheel motion traces, and full calibration. Notably, our multi-LiDAR fusion yields ~500K valid depth pixels per frame, about 6.5x more than KITTI Depth Completion and 10x more on average than other public driving datasets. The dataset spans ~110 km and 4.7 hours across Germany and Italy. In addition, CARD provides 2D bounding boxes targeting road-topography irregularities, enabling accurate benchmarking for both geometry and perception tasks. Furthermore, we establish a standardized evaluation protocol for road surface irregularities on CARD and benchmark state-of-the-art depth estimation models to provide strong baselines. The CARD dataset is hosted on https://huggingface.co/CARD-Data.

### [66] [Prompt-Anchored Vision-Text Distillation for Lifelong Person Re-identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05027)
*Wen Wen,Hao Chen,Shiliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 PAD（Prompt-Anchored vision-text Distillation），利用冻结的文本编码器作为稳定语义锚点，并结合视觉侧 EMA 教师与自适应提示池，缓解终身行人重识别中的语义漂移、适应性不足和灾难性遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 终身行人重识别需要模型在连续到来的多域数据上持续学习，但现有无样本方法多依赖纯视觉蒸馏或参数正则，难以同时保持旧知识稳定性与新域适应能力；同时，辅助文本模态在维持语义一致性方面的潜力尚未被充分利用。

Method: 提出非对称视觉-文本框架 PAD：文本侧使用预训练视觉-语言模型中的冻结文本编码器，并对 prompts 进行蒸馏，使其在固定语义空间中维持视觉-文本对齐，作为全局语义参考；视觉侧采用 EMA 教师模型和自适应 prompt pool，为新域分配新槽位，同时冻结旧槽位以保留历史知识。

Result: 大量实验表明，PAD 在已见域和未见域上均显著优于现有先进方法，并在稳定性与可塑性之间取得较好平衡。

Conclusion: 冻结文本编码器可作为跨域稳定语义锚点，结合提示蒸馏与视觉侧自适应机制，能够有效提升终身行人重识别模型的跨域泛化能力并减少遗忘。

Abstract: Lifelong person re-identification (LReID) aims to train a generalizable model with sequentially collected data. However, such models often suffer from semantic drift, limited adaptability, and catastrophic forgetting as new domains emerge. Existing exemplar-free approaches largely rely on visual-only distillation or parameter regularization, while overlooking the potential of auxiliary modalities, such as text, to preserve semantic stability and enable incremental plasticity. We observe that the frozen text encoder in pretrained vision-language models can serve as a stable semantic anchor across domains. To decouple the roles of vision and text, we propose Prompt-Anchored vision-text Distillation (PAD), an asymmetric vision-text framework for semantic alignment and cross-domain generalization. On the textual side, we distill prompts to preserve vision-text alignment under a fixed semantic space, acting as a global semantic reference rather than a dominant learning signal. On the visual side, an EMA-based teacher with an adaptive prompt pool enables domain-wise adaptation by allocating new slots while freezing past ones. Extensive experiments show that PAD substantially outperforms state-of-the-art methods across seen and unseen domains, achieving a strong balance between stability and plasticity. Project page is available at https://github.com/zu-zi/PAD.

### [67] [ScriptHOI: Learning Scripted State Transitions for Open-Vocabulary Human-Object Interaction Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05057)
*Minh Anh Nguyen,Quang Huy Tran,Bao Ngoc Le,SuiYang Guang,Tuan Kiet Pham,Linh Chi Vo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ScriptHOI 将开放词汇 HOI 短语建模为可分解的软脚本状态转移，通过状态槽匹配、冲突检测、区间式部分标签学习和反事实脚本对比，提升罕见/未见交互识别并减少由物体可供性导致的误报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言 HOI 检测器虽然能借助文本嵌入进行语义迁移，但预测常被物体可供性和短语共现关系主导，缺乏对手部、工具、目标、接触模式、几何关系、运动和物体状态等视觉证据的联合验证，导致开放词汇场景下出现错误交互预测。

Method: 提出 ScriptHOI，将每个交互短语分解为 body-role、contact、geometry、affordance、motion、object-state 等槽位；利用视觉状态 tokenizer 将人-物对解析为对应状态 token；通过槽级匹配估计 script coverage 与 script conflict，并用二者校准 HOI logits、暴露缺失证据、约束不完整标注训练；进一步采用 interval partial-label learning 为未标注候选设置脚本导出的概率上下界，避免闭世界负样本假设；使用 counterfactual script contrast loss 交换脚本槽位以抑制物体捷径。

Result: 在 HICO-DET、V-COCO 以及开放词汇 HOI 划分上的实验表明，ScriptHOI 提升了罕见与未见交互识别性能，并显著降低了可供性冲突导致的假阳性。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，将 HOI 短语从单一类别标签转化为结构化、可验证的状态转移脚本，有助于增强开放词汇泛化能力、提升视觉证据一致性，并缓解不完整标注与物体偏置问题。

Abstract: Open-vocabulary human-object interaction (HOI) detection requires recognizing interaction phrases that may not appear as annotated categories during training. Recent vision-language HOI detectors improve semantic transfer by matching human-object features with text embeddings, but their predictions are often dominated by object affordance and phrase-level co-occurrence. As a result, a model may predict \textit{cut cake} from the presence of a knife and a cake without verifying whether the hand, tool, target, contact pattern, and object state jointly support the action. We propose \textbf{ScriptHOI}, a structured framework that represents each interaction phrase as a soft scripted state transition. Rather than treating a phrase as a single class token, ScriptHOI decomposes it into body-role, contact, geometry, affordance, motion, and object-state slots. A visual state tokenizer parses each detected human-object pair into corresponding state tokens, and a slot-wise matcher estimates both script coverage and script conflict. These two quantities calibrate HOI logits, expose missing visual evidence, and provide training constraints for incomplete annotations. To avoid suppressing valid but unannotated interactions, we further introduce interval partial-label learning, which constrains unannotated candidates with script-derived lower and upper probability bounds instead of assigning closed-world negatives. A counterfactual script contrast loss swaps individual script slots to discourage object-only shortcuts. Experiments on HICO-DET, V-COCO, and open-vocabulary HOI splits show that ScriptHOI improves rare and unseen interaction recognition while substantially reducing affordance-conflict false positives.

</details>


### [68] [Height-Guided Projection Reparameterization for Camera-LiDAR Occupancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05072)
*Yuan Wu,Zhiqiang Yan,Jiawei Lian,Zhengxue Wang,Jian Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HiPR 通过利用 LiDAR 生成的 BEV 高度先验来自适应重参数化 2D-to-3D 投影空间，从而提升 3D 占用预测的几何对齐与特征聚合质量，并保持实时推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 3D occupancy 方法通常在固定投影空间中沿柱体均匀采样 3D 参考点，难以适应真实场景中的稀疏结构与高度变化，容易造成图像特征与体素位置之间的对应模糊和聚合不可靠。

Method: 提出 camera-LiDAR 框架 HiPR。首先将 LiDAR 编码为 BEV 高度图，用于表示点云最大高度；随后基于高度先验调整每个 pillar 的采样范围，实现高度引导的投影空间自适应重参数化，使投影点分布到更具几何意义的区域。同时，对高度图中的无效区域进行 mask，避免错误高度信息干扰特征聚合；训练阶段引入 Progressive Height Conditioning，逐步将条件信号从真实高度过渡到 LiDAR 高度，以缓解噪声高度导致的训练不稳定。

Result: 大量实验表明，HiPR 在 3D occupancy prediction 任务上稳定优于已有 SOTA 方法，同时仍能维持实时推理效率。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了显式高度先验对 2D-to-3D 视角转换具有重要价值。通过自适应投影重参数化与渐进式高度条件训练，HiPR 在准确性、几何一致性和推理效率之间取得了较好平衡。

Abstract: 3D occupancy prediction aims to infer dense, voxel-wise scene semantics from sensor observations, where the 2D-to-3D view transformation serves as a crucial step in bridging image features and volumetric representations. Most previous methods rely on a fixed projection space, where 3D reference points are uniformly sampled along pillars. However, such sampling struggles to capture the sparsity and height variations of real-world scenes, leading to ambiguous correspondences and unreliable feature aggregation. To address these challenges, we propose HiPR, a camera-LiDAR occupancy framework with Height-Guided Projection Reparameterization. HiPR first encodes LiDAR into a BEV height map to capture the maximum height of the point cloud. HiPR then adjusts the sampling range of each pillar using the height prior, enabling adaptive reparameterization of the projection space. As a result, the projected points are redistributed into geometrically meaningful regions rather than fixed ranges. Meanwhile, we mask out the invalid parts of the height map to avoid misleading the feature aggregation. In addition, to alleviate the training instability caused by noisy LiDAR-derived heights, we introduce a training-time Progressive Height Conditioning strategy, which gradually transitions the conditioning signal from ground-truth heights to LiDAR heights. Extensive experiments demonstrate that HiPR consistently outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods while maintaining real-time inference. The code and pretrained models can be found at https://github.com/Rayn-Wu/HiPR.

</details>

Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art approaches both with and without language guidance. ### [71] [Wasserstein-Aligned Localisation for VLM-Based Distributional OOD Detection in Medical Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05161)
*Bernhard Kainz,Johanna P Mueller,Matthew Baugh,Cosmin Bercea*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 WALDO：一种无需训练的零样本异常定位框架，通过与正常解剖参考分布进行结构化比较，提升视觉语言模型在稀有病理异常定位中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本异常定位依赖 VLM 的通用视觉-语言能力，但缺少“健康解剖结构”的上下文参照，导致难以准确判断哪些区域真正异常。作者希望将异常定位从单图判断转化为与正常参考样本分布的比较推理问题。

Method: WALDO 基于最优传输理论，使用 DINOv2 patch 表征构建正常解剖参考分布；通过熵加权 Sliced Wasserstein 距离进行解剖感知的参考选择；利用“Goldilocks zone”采样选择相似度适中的参考样本；最后通过加权非极大值抑制进行自一致性聚合。

Result: 在 NOVA 脑 MRI 基准上，WALDO 搭配 Qwen2.5-VL-72B 达到 43.5±1.6% mAP@30，相比零样本基线相对提升 19%。跨模型实验中，GPT-4o 和 Qwen3-VL-32B 均达到约 32.0% mAP@30；McNemar 配对检验显示结果具有统计显著性 p<0.01。

Conclusion: WALDO 表明，在零样本医学异常定位中，引入正常解剖参考并进行适度相似的比较推理，可以有效改善 VLM 的定位能力，且方法无需训练、具备跨模型泛化潜力。

Abstract: Zero-shot anomaly localisation via vision-language models (VLMs) offers a compelling approach for rare pathology detection, yet its performance is fundamentally limited by the absence of healthy anatomical context. We reformulate zero-shot localisation as a comparative inference problem in which anomalies are identified through structured comparison against reference distributions of normal anatomy. We introduce WALDO, a training-free framework grounded in optimal transport theory that enables comparative reasoning through: (i) entropy-weighted Sliced Wasserstein distances for anatomically-aware reference selection from DINOv2 patch distributions, (ii) Goldilocks zone sampling exploiting the non-monotonic relationship between reference similarity and localisation accuracy, and (iii) self-consistency aggregation via weighted non-maximum suppression. We theoretically analyse the Goldilocks effect through distributional divergence, and show that references with moderate similarity minimize a bias-variance trade-off in comparative visual reasoning. On the NOVA brain MRI benchmark, WALDO with Qwen2.5-VL-72B achieves $43.5_{\pm1.6}\%$ mAP@30 (95\% CI: [40.4, 46.7]), representing a 19\% relative improvement over zero-shot baselines. Cross-model evaluation shows consistent gains: GPT-4o achieves $32.0_{\pm6.5}\%$ and Qwen3-VL-32B achieves $32.0_{\pm6.6}\%$ mAP@30. Paired McNemar tests confirm statistical significance ($p<0.01$). Source code is available at https://github.com/bkainz/WALDO_MICCAI26_demo .

### [72] [OpenSearch-VL: An Open Recipe for Frontier Multimodal Search Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05185)

TL;DR: OpenSearch-VL 提供了一套完全开源的多模态深度搜索智能体训练方案，通过高质量数据构建、统一工具环境和改进的多轮强化学习算法，在多个基准上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前前沿多模态搜索智能体具备主动搜索、证据验证和多步推理能力，但难以复现，主要原因是缺乏开放的高质量训练数据、透明的轨迹合成流程以及详细训练配方。论文旨在降低复现门槛，支持开放研究。

Method: 作者提出 OpenSearch-VL：首先通过 Wikipedia 路径采样、模糊实体改写和源锚视觉定位构建训练数据，以减少捷径学习和一步检索坍塌；随后构建 SearchVL-SFT-36k 和 SearchVL-RL-8k 两个数据集；同时设计包含文本搜索、图像搜索、OCR、裁剪、锐化、超分辨率和透视校正的多样化工具环境；最后提出多轮 fatal-aware GRPO 算法，通过屏蔽失败后的 token 并使用单侧优势截断保留失败前有效推理。

Abstract: Deep search has become a crucial capability for frontier multimodal agents, enabling models to solve complex questions through active search, evidence verification, and multi-step reasoning. Despite rapid progress, top-tier multimodal search agents remain difficult to reproduce, largely due to the absence of open high-quality training data, transparent trajectory synthesis pipelines, or detailed training recipes. To this end, we introduce OpenSearch-VL, a fully open-source recipe for training frontier multimodal deep search agents with agentic reinforcement learning. First, we curated a dedicated pipeline to construct high-quality training data through Wikipedia path sampling, fuzzy entity rewriting, and source-anchor visual grounding, which jointly reduce shortcuts and one-step retrieval collapse. Based on this pipeline, we curate two training datasets, SearchVL-SFT-36k for SFT and SearchVL-RL-8k for RL. Besides, we design a diverse tool environment that unifies text search, image search, OCR, cropping, sharpening, super-resolution, and perspective correction, enabling agents to combine active perception with external knowledge acquisition. Finally, we propose a multi-turn fatal-aware GRPO training algorithm that handles cascading tool failures by masking post-failure tokens while preserving useful pre-failure reasoning through one-sided advantage clamping. Built on this recipe, OpenSearch-VL delivers substantial performance gains, with over 10-point average improvements across seven benchmarks, and achieves results comparable to proprietary commercial models on several tasks. We will release all data, code, and models to support open research on multimodal deep search agents.

### [74] [D-OPSD: On-Policy Self-Distillation for Continuously Tuning Step-Distilled Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05204)
*Dengyang Jiang,Xin Jin,Dongyang Liu,Zanyi Wang,Mingzhe Zheng,Ruoyi Du,Xiangpeng Yang,Qilong Wu,Zhen Li,Peng Gao,Harry Yang,Steven Hoi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出 D-OPSD，将训练设计为 on-policy 自蒸馏过程。模型同时扮演教师和学生：学生仅基于文本特征条件化，教师基于文本提示与目标图像构成的多模态特征条件化。训练在学生自身 rollout 轨迹上，最小化教师与学生预测分布之间的差异。

Result: 该方法使模型能够在自身生成轨迹和自身监督信号下学习新概念、风格等，同时保持原始少步推理能力。

Abstract: The landscape of high-performance image generation models is currently shifting from the inefficient multi-step ones to the efficient few-step counterparts (e.g, Z-Image-Turbo and FLUX.2-klein). However, these models present significant challenges for directly continuous supervised fine-tuning. For example, applying the commonly used fine-tuning technique would compromises their inherent few-step inference capability. To address this, we propose D-OPSD, a novel training paradigm for step-distilled diffusion models that enables on-policy learning during supervised fine-tuning. We first find that the modern diffusion model where the LLM/VLM serves as the encoder can inherit its encoder's in-context capabilities. This enables us to make the training as an on-policy self-distillation process. Specifically, during training, we make the model acts as both the teacher and the student with different contexts, where the student is conditioned only on the text feature, while the teacher is conditioned on the multimodal feature of both the text prompt and the target image. Training minimizes the two predicted distributions over the student's own roll-outs. By optimized on the model's own trajectory and under it's own supervision, D-OPSD enables the model to learn new concept, style, etc. without sacrificing the original few-step capacity.

*Zeren Jiang,Yushi Lan,Yihang Luo,Yufan Deng,Zihang Lai,Edgar Sucar,Christian Rupprecht,Iro Laina,Diane Larlus,Chuanxia Zheng,Andrea Vedaldi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Syn4D 是一个面向动态场景的多视角合成数据集，提供相机运动、深度、密集跟踪与人体姿态等高质量标注，用于推动单目视频中的稠密 3D/4D 重建与动态场景理解研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单目视频动态场景的稠密 3D 重建与跟踪仍是计算机视觉中的开放难题，主要受限于缺乏具备稠密、完整、准确几何标注的高质量数据集。

Method: 作者提出 Syn4D 多视角合成动态场景数据集，提供真实值相机运动、深度图、密集点跟踪和参数化人体姿态标注；其核心能力是支持将任意像素反投影到任意时间和任意相机视角下的 3D 空间。

Result: 作者在多个下游任务上进行评估，包括 4D 场景重建、3D 点跟踪、几何感知相机重定向和人体姿态估计，实验显示该数据集具有良好的实用性和有效性。

Conclusion: Syn4D 有望缓解动态场景几何标注稀缺的问题，并促进动态场景理解、时空建模及相关 3D/4D 视觉任务的发展。

Abstract: Dense 3D reconstruction and tracking of dynamic scenes from monocular video remains an important open challenge in computer vision. Progress in this area has been constrained by the scarcity of high-quality datasets with dense, complete, and accurate geometric annotations. To address this limitation, we introduce Syn4D, a multiview synthetic dataset of dynamic scenes that includes ground-truth camera motion, depth maps, dense tracking, and parametric human pose annotations. A key feature of Syn4D is the ability to unproject any pixel into 3D to any time and to any camera. We conduct extensive evaluations across multiple downstream tasks to demonstrate the utility and effectiveness of the proposed dataset, including 4D scene reconstruction, 3D point tracking, geometry-aware camera retargeting, and human pose estimation. The experimental results highlight Syn4D's potential to facilitate research in dynamic scene understanding and spatiotemporal modeling.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 任务要求检测多编程语言、多应用场景下的机器生成代码，并需要系统能够泛化到未见过的语言和领域；大型预训练代码模型成本较高，因此需要更轻量、计算效率更高的替代方案。

Method: 作者探索预训练代码编码器与轻量特征方法，重点设计对代码片段长度不敏感的比例型特征；借助解析引擎和编程语言分类器提取与描述性相关的信号；另外训练代码-文本行分类器，用于识别样本中嵌入的自然语言片段；最终结合浅层决策树和基于数据分析得到的启发式规则进行预测。

Result: 该方法仅需 CPU 训练，推理几乎即时，计算效率高；摘要未给出具体排行榜名次或量化性能指标。

Conclusion: 论文表明，面向机器生成代码检测，精心设计的轻量特征与简单模型结合启发式规则，可以在资源消耗极低的情况下提供一种可行的替代方案，尤其适合对部署效率要求较高的场景。

Abstract: SemEval-2026 Task 13 investigates machine-generated code detection across multiple programming languages and application scenarios, asking participating systems to generalize to unseen languages and domains. This paper describes our participation in Subtask A (binary classification) and explores both pretrained code encoders and lightweight feature-based methods. We design ratio-based features that are less sensitive to snippet length. To support the extraction of descriptiveness-related signals, we use parsing engines and a programming-language classifier. Additionally, we train a separate code-vs-text line classifier to identify raw natural language segments embedded within samples. We combine a shallow decision tree with heuristic rules derived from data analysis to produce the final predictions. Our approach is computationally efficient, requires only CPU resources for training, and achieves near-instant inference time, offering a lightweight alternative to large pretrained models.

### [78] [Not All That Is Fluent Is Factual: Investigating Hallucinations of Large Language Models in Academic Writing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04171)
*Humam Khan,Md Tabrez Nafis,Shahab Saquib Sohail,Aqeel Khalique,Rehan Hasan Khan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文评估四种主流大语言模型在学术写作任务中的幻觉表现，并提出加权指标 Hallucination Index（HI）进行量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM 在学术内容生成中虽能力突出，但容易产生事实错误、无效引用、风格不一致等幻觉问题；现有评估指标对某些会改变语义或情感的错误识别不足，因此需要面向学术写作场景的系统评估。

Method: 研究选取 ChatGPT、Grok、Gemini 和 Copilot，设计 80 个提示，覆盖参考文献生成、事实解释、摘要生成和写作润色四类任务；使用 0–5 分量表从事实准确性、引用有效性、连贯性、风格一致性和学术语气等维度评分，并提出加权 Hallucination Index 衡量模型输出中的幻觉程度。

Result: Grok 和 Copilot 在参考文献生成任务上表现较好，但在摘要或风格类提示中较弱，HI 分别为 0.67 和 0.70；Gemini 和 ChatGPT 在语气控制方面较强，但在事实性任务中不足，幻觉风险较高，HI 分别为 0.53 和 0.57。

Conclusion: LLM 的幻觉行为不仅取决于模型架构，也受任务类型和提示条件影响；该研究为未来学术写作场景下的幻觉评估与缓解提供了新的研究方向。

Abstract: Large Language models (LLMs) show extraordinary abilities, but they are still prone to hallucinations, especially when we use them for generating Academic content. We have investigated four popular LLMs, ChatGPT, Grok, Gemini, and Copilot for hallucinations specifically for academic writing. We have designed 80 prompts across four categories, namely, reference generation, factual explanation, abstract generation, and writing improvement. We evaluated the model using a 0-5 rubric score, which checks factual accuracy, reference validity, coherence, style consistency, and academic tone. A novel weighted metric, Hallucination Index (HI), was introduced to measure hallucination in the responses generated by the models. Some of the most widely used evaluation metrics often fail to check errors which alter sentiment in machine-translated text. We found that Grok and Copilot perform better on reference generation tasks, but they often struggle with abstract or stylistic prompts, with HI values of 0.67 and 0.70, respectively. Whereas, Gemini and ChatGPT have done well with having stronger tone control, but they lack in writing factual tasks and higher hallucination risk with HI scores of 0.53 and 0.57, respectively. Our study found that hallucination behavior does not depend solely on model architecture but also on the type of task and the prompting conditions we are providing. We propose that our work opens new research dimensions for future researchers.

</details>


### [79] [Are LLMs Ready for Conflict Monitoring? Empirical Evidence from West Africa](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04177)
*Hoffmann Muki,Olukunle Owolabi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型用于冲突事件监测时存在系统性偏差：通用开源模型更易将合法战斗误判为针对平民的暴力，领域适配模型在方向性偏差上更中性，但仍存在显著的行为体选择偏差与语境相关风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM被用于冲突监测，若其输出存在系统性失真，可能影响人道问责与事件分类可信度。因此需要评估不同模型在冲突事件分类中的规范性偏差、行为体偏差和对地理语境词汇扰动的鲁棒性。

Method: 论文比较四个通用开源权重模型与两个领域适配模型，在尼日利亚和喀麦隆冲突事件分类任务上，以ACLED多阶段验证数据集为金标准；分析错误方向、合法化/非法化偏差、行为体偏差、词汇扰动翻转率，并进行错误轨迹与理由忠实性剖析。

Result: 通用模型表现出显著的错误非法化偏差，例如Gemma将18.29%的合法战斗误分为针对平民暴力且无错误合法化；领域适配模型方向性偏差接近零。但适配模型仍有显著行为体偏差，如尼日利亚相同战术情境下国家行为体比非国家行为体被合法化的比例高36.5%。通用模型对地域性词汇框架敏感，翻转率最高达66.7%，且理由解释存在虚构；适配模型对扰动更稳健。

Conclusion: 当前模型尚不适合在冲突监测中无监督部署。研究建议采用公平性感知微调、强制性对抗鲁棒性评估，并结合地区难度设置有针对性的人类监督流程。

Abstract: As LLMs enter conflict monitoring, understanding systematic distortions in their outputs is critical for humanitarian accountability. We evaluate four vanilla open-weight models Gemma 3 4B, Llama 3.2 3B, Mistral 7B, and OLMo 2 7B and two domain-adapted models, AfroConfliBERT and AfroConfliLLAMA, on Nigeria and Cameroon conflict-event classification against ACLED, a gold-standard dataset with multi-stage verification. We find a bifurcated divergence in normative directionality. Open-weight models exhibit statistically significant False Illegitimation bias: Gemma misclassifies to 18.29% of legitimate battles as civilian-targeted violence while making zero False Legitimation errors. By contrast, AfroConfliBERT and AfroConfliLLAMA achieve near-directional neutrality, with Legitimization Bias differences indistinguishable from zero. Yet domain adaptation does not eliminate actor-based selection bias. Both adapted models show statistically significant actor bias comparable to vanilla LLMs; in Nigeria, state actors are legitimized 36.5% more often than non-state actors in identical tactical contexts. Open-weight outputs are also fragile to geography-specific lexical framing: delegitimizing phrases produce flip rates up to 66.7% in Cameroon and 34.2% in Nigeria, while perturbations salient in one context may not matter in another. Error trace profiling shows models mask normative bias through unfaithful rationale confabulations. In contrast, AfroConfliBERT and AfroConfliLLAMA are largely robust, with near-zero flip rates across perturbation categories. Overall, current models are not ready for unsupervised deployment in conflict monitoring. We call for fairness-aware fine-tuning to reduce actor-based selection bias, mandatory adversarial robustness evaluation against lexical manipulation, and context-specific human-in-the-loop oversight calibrated to regional difficulty.

</details>


### [80] [MedFabric and EtHER: A Data-Centric Framework for Word-Level Fabrication Generation and Detection in Medical LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04180)
*Tung Sum Thomas Kwok,Qian Qian,Xiaofeng Lin,Dongxu Zhang,Jun Han,Zhichao Yang,Davin Hill,Tamer Soliman,Sanjit Singh Batra,Robert Tillman,Guang Cheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出面向医疗文本的细粒度事实捏造数据集 MedFabric，并基于此设计模块化词级捏造检测器 ETHER，用于提升医疗领域事实一致性检测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在医疗等专业领域容易产生流畅但事实错误的内容；现有医疗幻觉数据集对“捏造”现象覆盖不足，且存在人工文本与模型文本风格差异、合成幻觉样本分布漂移等问题，难以支撑可靠检测。

Method: 作者构建数据中心流水线，生成保持句法与文体一致但引入细微事实偏差的词级医疗捏造样本，形成 MedFabric；随后提出 ETHER，结合 Text2Table 分解、词遮蔽与填充、混合句对评估等模块进行词级事实对齐与捏造检测。

Result: 实验表明，基于 MedFabric/ETHER 的方法在词级捏造检测基准上较当前先进检测器提升超过 15%，并且在不同结构相似度条件下保持稳定表现。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个更贴近真实医疗捏造现象的数据集与检测框架，有助于提升专业领域大语言模型输出的事实性审查与安全可靠性。

Abstract: Large Language Models exhibit strong reasoning and semantic understanding capabilities but often hallucinate in domains that require expert knowledge, among which fabrications, the generation of factually incorrect yet fluent statements, pose the greatest risk in medical contexts. Existing medical hallucination datasets inadequately capture fabrication phenomena due to limited fabrication coverage, stylistic disparities between human and LLM-authored texts, and distributional drift during hallucinated sample synthesis. To address this, we propose a data-centric pipeline to generate realistic and word-level fabrications that preserve syntactic and stylistic fidelity while introducing subtle factual deviations, resulting in MedFabric. Building upon this dataset, we introduce ETHER, a modular word-level fabrication detector integrating Text2Table Decomposition, Word Masking and Filling and Hybrid Sentence Pair Evaluation to enhance factual alignment. Empirical results demonstrate that MedFabric outperforms state-of-the-art detectors by over 15% on word-level fabrication benchmarks while maintaining consistent performance across structural similarities, offering a comprehensive framework for reliable and domain-specific factuality detection.

</details>


### [81] [The Impact of Vocabulary Overlaps on Knowledge Transfer in Multilingual Machine Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04196)
*Oona Itkonen,Jörg Tiedemann*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过系统比较联合词表与非联合词表、相关与不相关辅助语言，在域外多语言神经机器翻译设置中研究知识迁移来源，发现词表重叠有帮助，但领域匹配和语言相关性更关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多语言神经机器翻译中跨语言知识迁移已被证明有效，但联合词表带来的词汇重叠究竟在多大程度上贡献了迁移效果仍缺乏共识；非联合词表对性能的影响也研究不足。

Method: 作者设计域外实验以突出迁移效应，系统比较联合词表与非联合词表，并引入与源语言相关及不相关的辅助语言，评估不同条件下MNMT模型表现。

Result: 实验显示，相关语言通常因更高词表重叠获得更好结果；但即使词表设置变化，领域匹配和语言相关性对性能的影响大于是否使用联合词表。

Conclusion: MNMT中的知识迁移并不主要由联合词表或词汇重叠单独决定；选择领域匹配、语言相关的辅助数据比单纯依赖联合词表更重要。

Abstract: Knowledge transfer, especially across related languages, has been found beneficial for multilingual neural machine translation (MNMT), but some aspects are still under-explored and deserve further investigation. A joint vocabulary is most often applied to form a uniform word embedding space, but since the impact of a disjoint vocabulary on model performance is far less studied, there is no consensus on how much knowledge transfer is mainly due to vocabulary overlap. In this paper, we present systematic experiments with joint and disjoint vocabularies, and auxiliary languages related and unrelated to the source language. We design this experiment in an out-of-domain setup in order to emphasize transfer and the impact of the auxiliary language. As expected, we yield better results with more extensive vocabulary overlaps typical for related languages, but our experiments also show that domain-match and language relatedness are more important than a joint vocabulary.

</details>


### [82] [Nsanku: Evaluating Zero-Shot Translation Performance of LLMs for Ghanaian Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04208)
*Stephen E. Moore,Mich-Seth Owusu,Akwasi Asare,Lawrence Adu Gyamfi,Paul Azunre,Joel Budu,Jonathan Asiamah,Elias Dzobo,Kelvin Newman,Edmund O. Benefo,Gerhardt Datsomor,Onesimus Addo Appiah,Ama Branoa Banful,Lucas Woedem Kpatah,Saani Mustapha Deishini,John Ayernor*

TL;DR: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Result: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Conclusion: This content has not passed the compliance test and has been hidden.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive multilingual capabilities for well-resourced languages, yet their performance on low-resource African languages remains poorly understood and largely unevaluated. This paper presents Nsanku, a systematic benchmark that evaluates the zero-shot machine translation performance of 19 open-weight and proprietary LLMs across 43 Ghanaian languages paired with English. Evaluation sentences were sourced from the YouVersion Bible platform, providing 300 sentence pairs per language. Two complementary automatic metrics are employed: Bilingual Evaluation Understudy (BLEU) and Character n-gram F-Score (chrF), alongside an average accuracy score and a cross-language consistency dimension. Nsanku represents the most comprehensive LLM translation evaluation for Ghanaian languages conducted to date. Results show that gemini-2.5-flash achieves the highest overall average score of 26.88 (BLEU: 24.60, chrF: 29.16), followed by claude-sonnet-4-5 at 24.87 (BLEU: 22.46, chrF: 27.28) and gpt-4.1 at 23.20 (BLEU: 21.15, chrF: 25.24). Among open-weight models, kimi-k2-instruct-0905 leads at an average score of 20.87. A critical finding from the consistency analysis is that no model and no language reached the Leaders quadrant of high performance and high consistency simultaneously, indicating that current LLMs are not yet reliably usable for Ghanaian language translation at scale. Siwu achieved the highest per-language average score at 25.73 while Nkonya scored lowest at 11.65. Nsanku establishes a publicly available, community-extensible evaluation infrastructure for African language NLP research.

</details>


### [83] [Self-Prompting Small Language Models for Privacy-Sensitive Clinical Information Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04221)
*Yao-Shun Chuang,Tushti Mody,Uday Pratap Singh,Shirindokht Shiraz,Chun-Teh Lee,Ryan Brandon,Muhammad F Walji,Xiaoqian Jiang,Bunmi Tokede*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 牙科病程记录高度非结构化、领域术语密集且涉及隐私，传统通用模型或依赖云端的大模型难以直接、安全、稳定地用于临床实体抽取，因此需要面向任务的本地化、可扩展方法。

Method: 研究使用1,200条标注牙科记录评估开放权重小语言模型；框架让模型自生成、校验、细化和评估不同临床实体的提示词；采用多提示集成推理，并对表现较好的模型进行QLoRA监督微调和直接偏好优化（DPO）。

Result: 模型性能差异显著，说明通用基准不能替代任务特定评估。Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct基线表现最佳。经过DPO后，Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct达到micro/macro F1为0.864/0.837，Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct达到0.806/0.797。

Conclusion: 自动化提示优化结合轻量级偏好后训练，可提升本地部署小语言模型在临床信息抽取中的可扩展性和有效性，尤其适用于隐私敏感的牙科临床文本场景。

Abstract: Clinical named entity recognition from dental progress notes is challenging because documentation is highly unstructured, domain-specific, and often privacy-sensitive. We developed a locally deployable framework that enables small language models to self-generate, verify, refine, and evaluate entity-specific prompts for extracting multiple clinical entities from dental notes. Using 1,200 annotated notes, we evaluated candidate open-weight models with multi-prompt ensemble inference and further adapted selected models using QLoRA-based supervised fine-tuning and direct preference optimization. Model performance varied substantially, highlighting the need for task-specific evaluation rather than reliance on generic benchmarks. Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct achieved the strongest baseline performance. After DPO, Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct achieved micro/macro F1 scores of 0.864/0.837 and 0.806/0.797, respectively. These findings suggest that automated prompt optimization combined with lightweight preference-based post-training can support scalable clinical information extraction using locally deployed small language models.

### [84] [Material Database Agent: A Multimodal Agentic Framework for Scientific Literature Mining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04278)

TL;DR: 本文提出 Material Database Agent（MDA），一种模块化多智能体系统，可从论文 PDF 中并行抽取文本与图像信息，并自动汇总为材料科学结构化数据库。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料科学研究高度依赖文献中的结构化与非结构化数据，但大量实验细节分散在正文、表格、图表和图片中，传统人工建库耗时、难扩展；随着多模态大语言模型的发展，自动化、高准确率的信息抽取成为可能。

Method: MDA 以论文 PDF 为输入，将其并行处理为 markdown 文件和图像；多个子智能体分别读取文本与图像信息，为每篇论文构建子数据库；随后由汇总智能体将各子数据库整合为统一的表格数据库。该方法区别于规则系统或单轮抽取流水线，采用面向材料科学数据库构建的模块化多智能体架构。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了多模态智能体式信息抽取可作为从原始科学文献构建下一代科学数据库的可行路径，尤其适用于材料科学领域的大规模数据库建设。

Abstract: Materials science workflows rely on structured and unstructured data from the vast body of available scientific literature. However, most of the experimental details remain buried in text, tables, graphs and figures. Thus, constructing databases that incorporate this data is a manual, time-consuming, and hard-to-scale process. Multimodal large language models have made it feasible to extract information from text and scientific figures with high speed and accuracy. This opens the possibility of an AI system that can create production-scale material databases. Material Database Agent (MDA) is a modular, multi-agent system architecture for converting research literature into structured databases. MDA accepts article PDFs as input, which are subsequently processed in parallel into markdown files and figures. Multiple sub-agents read these markdown files and figures in parallel to assemble sub-databases for each paper. These sub-databases are then compiled into a single tabular database by an agent. As opposed to using either a rule-based approach or a single-pass pipeline for extracting information, MDA is a specialized architecture for transforming the literature into a database in the field of materials science. More generally, this study provides a basis for positioning multimodal agentic information extraction as a viable means for constructing next-generation scientific databases from the primary literature.

### [85] [Towards Self-Referential Analytic Assessment: A Profile-Based Approach to L2 Writing Evaluation with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04298)

Abstract: Automated essay scoring (AES) research often relies on rank-based correlation metrics to validate analytic assessment. As a result, high correlations may mask a system's true diagnostic behaviour. To obtain reliable reference scores, we apply two-facet Rasch modelling to calibrate rater severity and derive fair average scores across ten analytic aspects and holistic proficiency. We compare the analytic scoring performance of human operational raters and three large language models (LLMs) in a zero-shot setting. Our results show that LLMs tend to outperform single human raters in identifying relative weaknesses (negative feedback) across several proficiency aspects, while human raters remain stronger at identifying relative strengths (positive feedback). Overall, our findings highlight the limitations of rank-based evaluation for analytic assessment and demonstrate the value of intra-learner, profile-based methods for assessing and deploying LLMs in AES.

### [86] [SWAN: Semantic Watermarking with Abstract Meaning Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04305)
*Ziping Ye,Gourab Dey,Christos Christodoulopoulos,Charith Peris,Anil Ramakrishna,Weitong Ruan,Aram Galstyan,Kai-Wei Chang,Rahul Gupta,Ninareh Mehrabi*

TL;DR: SWAN 将水印签名嵌入句子的 AMR 语义结构，而非生成时的词元选择偏好，从而在保义改写下保持水印可检测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本水印方法多依赖词元级生成偏置，面对同义改写或释义攻击时容易失效；因此需要一种更贴近语义层、能随意义保持而保留的鲁棒文本溯源机制。

Method: 提出 SWAN 框架：选择携带签名的 AMR 模板，通过提示 LLM 在保持上下文连贯的同时生成符合该语义结构的句子；检测阶段使用现成 AMR 解析器提取语义结构，并采用单比例 z 检验判断水印存在性。该方法无需训练。

Result: 在 RealNews 基准上的实验显示，SWAN 在未被篡改的水印文本上达到与当前先进方法相当的检测性能；在改写场景下显著更鲁棒，相比既有方法检测 AUC 最高提升 13.9 个百分点。

Abstract: We introduce SWAN (Semantic Watermarking with Abstract Meaning Representation), a novel framework that embeds watermark signatures into the semantic structure of a sentence using Abstract Meaning Representation (AMR). In contrast to existing watermarking methods, which typically encode signatures by adjusting token selection preferences during text generation, SWAN embeds the signature directly in the sentence's semantic representation. As the signature is encoded at the semantic structure level, any paraphrase that preserves meaning automatically preserves the signature. SWAN is training-free: watermark injection is achieved by prompting an LLM to generate sentences guided by a selected AMR template while maintaining contextual coherence, and detection uses an off-the-shelf AMR parser followed by a simple one-proportion z-test. Empirical evaluation on the RealNews benchmark shows SWAN matches state-of-the-art detection performance on unaltered watermarked text, while significantly improving robustness against paraphrasing, increasing detection AUC by up to 13.9 percentage points compared to prior methods. These results demonstrate that SWAN's approach of anchoring watermarks in AMR semantic structures provides a simple, effective, and prompt-based method for robust text provenance verification under paraphrasing, opening new avenues for semantic-level watermarking research.

### [87] [NoisyCausal: A Benchmark for Evaluating Causal Reasoning Under Structured Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04313)
*Zhi Xu,Yun Fu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 NoisyCausal 基准，用于评估大语言模型在结构化噪声下的自然语言因果推理能力，并提出结合显式因果结构与 LLM 的模块化推理框架，实验显示其优于常规提示与推理基线，且能泛化到外部基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言因果推理需要识别变量、理解变量交互，并在噪声、歧义、无关信息或部分错误观测下推断效应与干预。现有 LLM 虽具备较强通用推理能力，但在区分相关性与因果性、处理干扰信息和不完整观测方面仍存在明显不足，因此需要更有针对性的评测基准和推理方法。

Method: 作者构建 NoisyCausal 基准：每个样本从真实因果图生成，并映射为自然语言场景，同时注入可控结构化噪声，包括无关干扰项、数值扰动、混杂因素和部分可观测性。方法上，提出模块化推理框架：先提示 LLM 从上下文中抽取变量并构建因果图，再将原始推理任务重写为基于该图结构的结构化提示，使 LLM 在显式符号因果结构约束下完成推理。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在 NoisyCausal 上显著优于标准提示方法和其他推理基线；同时，在无需任务特定微调的情况下，能够较好泛化到 Cladder 等外部因果推理基准。

Conclusion: 研究表明，将因果抽象、显式图结构与语言模型推理结合，有助于提升 LLM 在噪声自然语言场景中的因果理解能力，使推理过程更稳健、可解释且更接近真实因果推断。

Abstract: Causal reasoning in natural language requires identifying relevant variables, understanding their interactions, and reasoning about effects and interventions, often under noisy or ambiguous conditions. While large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong general reasoning abilities, they struggle to disentangle correlation from causation, particularly when observations are partially incorrect or irrelevant information is present. In this work, we introduce NoisyCausal, a new benchmark designed to evaluate causal reasoning under structured noise. Each instance is generated from a ground-truth causal graph and contextualized with a natural language scenario by injecting controllable forms of noise, such as irrelevant distractors, value perturbations, confounding, and partial observability. Moreover, we propose a modular reasoning framework that combines LLMs with explicit causal structure to address these challenges. Our method prompts the LLM to extract variables, construct a causal graph from context, and then reformulates the reasoning task as a structured prompt grounded in this graph. Rather than relying on statistical patterns alone, the LLM is guided by symbolic structure, enabling more interpretable and robust inference. Experimental results show that our method significantly outperforms standard prompting and reasoning baselines on NoisyCausal. Furthermore, it generalizes well to external benchmarks such as Cladder without task-specific tuning. Our findings highlight the importance of combining causal abstractions with language-driven reasoning to achieve faithful and robust causal understanding in LLMs.

### [88] [Telegraph English: Semantic Prompt Compression via Structured Symbolic Rewriting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04426)
*Mikhail L. Arbuzov,Sisong Bei,Ziwei Dong,Dmitri Kalaev,Alexey A. Shvets*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 Telegraph English（TE），一种将自然语言重写为符号化、结构化事实行的提示压缩协议，在约 50% token 压缩下仍能高保真保留关键信息，并优于 LLMLingua-2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于 token 删除的提示压缩方法通常按固定比例移除低重要性词，可能破坏语义关系与细节信息。作者希望通过完整语义重写，在减少 token 的同时保留事实、关系和可寻址结构。

Method: TE 将输入分解为原子事实行，用约 40 个逻辑与关系符号替换冗长短语，并根据文档信息密度自适应压缩比例。其行结构使每一行成为独立可索引事实，从而把压缩与语义分块合并为同一过程。实验在 LongBench-v2 的 4,081 个问答对上进行，覆盖五个 OpenAI 模型和两个难度层级，并与 LLMLingua-2 在匹配压缩率下比较。

Result: 在约 50% token 减少时，TE 在 GPT-4.1 上对关键事实保持 99.1% 准确率；在所有测试模型和任务上均优于 LLMLingua-2。小模型上的优势更明显，在细粒度任务中最高提升 11 个百分点。

Conclusion: TE 表明，显式关系结构和语义化重写比简单 token 删除更能维持压缩后提示的可用性，尤其能弥补小模型容量有限的问题。作者还发布了语法规范、压缩提示、基准数据和参考实现。

Abstract: We introduce Telegraph English (TE), a prompt-compression protocol that rewrites natural language into a symbol-rich, formally-structured dialect. Where token-deletion methods such as LLMLingua-2 train a classifier to delete low-importance tokens at a fixed ratio, TE performs a full semantic rewrite: it decomposes the input into atomic fact lines, substitutes verbose phrases with $\sim$40 logical and relational symbols, and lets the compression ratio adapt to each document's information density. A consequence of the line-structure rule is that compression and semantic chunking become the same operation -- each output line is an independently addressable fact, so the compressed representation is simultaneously a semantic index. We evaluate TE on 4{,}081 question-answer pairs from LongBench-v2 across five OpenAI models and two difficulty levels. At roughly 50\% token reduction, TE preserves 99.1\% accuracy on key facts with GPT-4.1 and outperforms LLMLingua-2 at matched compression ratios on every model and task tested. The gap widens on smaller models -- up to 11 percentage points on fine-detail tasks -- suggesting that explicit relational structure compensates for limited model capacity. We release the grammar specification, compression prompt, benchmark data, and reference implementation.

### [89] [DoGMaTiQ: Automated Generation of Question-and-Answer Nuggets for Report Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04458)
*Bryan Li,William Walden,Yu Hou,Gabrielle Kaili-May Liu,Dawn Lawrie,Jame Mayfield,Eugene Yang,Chris Callison-Burch,Laura Dietz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 DoGMaTiQ：一种自动生成 QA 形式 nugget 集并用于跨语言长报告评估的流水线，在 TREC NeuCLIR 与 RAGTIME 任务上与人工评判具有较强相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG 系统生成的长篇、带引用报告需要细粒度评估。传统 nugget 需要人工为每个主题构建，成本高、扩展性差；在跨语言场景中，多语文档来源进一步加剧了这一问题。因此需要一种自动、高质量、可扩展的 QA-based nugget 构建方法。

Method: 作者提出三阶段流水线 DoGMaTiQ：首先基于源文档生成文档支撑的 QA nugget；其次对语义等价或近似的改写进行聚类；最后依据明确的质量准则进行 nugget 子集筛选。随后将生成的 nugget 集接入 AutoArgue 评估框架，实现对生成报告的全自动 nugget-based 评价。

Result: 在两个跨语言 TREC 共享任务 NeuCLIR 和 RAGTIME 上，实验显示 DoGMaTiQ 驱动的自动评估与 human-in-the-loop 以及完全人工判断之间具有较强的系统排序相关性。分析还表明，强大的 LLM nugget 生成器是性能关键，且由 DoGMaTiQ 得到的系统排名对异常系统较为鲁棒。

Conclusion: DoGMaTiQ 有效降低了跨语言 RAG 报告评估中人工构建 nugget 的成本，并能产生与人工评估高度一致的自动评价结果。该工作为可扩展、细粒度、跨语言的长报告评估提供了实用方案，并通过公开代码和数据促进后续研究。

Abstract: Evaluation of long-form, citation-backed reports has lately received significant attention due to the wide-scale adoption of retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems. Core to many evaluation frameworks is the use of atomic facts, or nuggets, to assess a report's coverage of query-relevant information attested in the underlying collection. While nuggets have traditionally been represented as short statements, recent work has used question-answer (QA) representations, enabling fine-grained evaluations that decouple the information need (i.e. the question) from the potentially diverse content that satisfies it (i.e. its answers).
  A persistent challenge for nugget-based evaluation is the need to manually curate sets of nuggets for each topic in a test collection -- a laborious process that scales poorly to novel information needs. This challenge is acute in cross-lingual settings, where information is found in multilingual source documents. Accordingly, we introduce DoGMaTiQ, a pipeline for generating high-quality QA-based nugget sets in three stages: (1) document-grounded nugget generation, (2) paraphrase clustering, and (3) nugget subselection based on principled quality criteria. We integrate DoGMaTiQ nuggets with AutoArgue -- a recent nugget-based evaluation framework -- to enable fully automatic evaluation of generated reports. We conduct extensive experiments on two cross-lingual TREC shared tasks, NeuCLIR and RAGTIME, showing strong rank correlations with both human-in-the-loop and fully manual judgments. Finally, detailed analysis of our pipeline reveals that a strong LLM nugget generator is key, and that the system rankings induced by DoGMaTiQ are robust to outlier systems. We facilitate future research in report evaluation by publicly releasing our code and artifacts at https://github.com/manestay/dogmatiq.

### [90] [CAR: Query-Guided Confidence-Aware Reranking for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04495)
*Zhipeng Song,Yizhi Zhou,Xiangyu Kong,Jiulong Jiao,Xuezhou Ye,Chunqi Gao,Xueqing Shi,Yuhang Zhou,Heng Qi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CAR提出一种训练免费、即插即用的置信度感知重排序框架，用生成器置信度变化衡量文档对RAG生成的实际有用性，并在多个检索器、重排序器和LLM上提升NDCG@5，且排序收益与下游生成F1高度相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统RAG重排序主要优化查询—文档相关性，但相关文档不一定能帮助生成，甚至可能引入噪声；相反，排名较低的文档可能更能降低生成器不确定性。因此需要一种直接面向生成有用性的文档排序信号。

Method: CAR通过比较查询单独输入与查询+文档输入条件下，多次采样答案之间的语义一致性来估计生成器置信度变化。若文档显著提升置信度则上调排名，降低置信度则下调排名，不确定时保持基线顺序；同时使用查询级门控机制，避免对本已高置信度的查询进行不必要干预。

Result: 在四个BEIR数据集上，CAR在稀疏/稠密检索器、LLM重排序器/监督重排序器以及四种LLM骨干上均稳定提升NDCG@5。尤其在Contriever检索下，CAR使YesNo重排序器平均提升25.4%；其排序增益与下游生成F1改进高度相关，Spearman rho达到0.964。

Conclusion: CAR表明，利用生成器置信度变化可以更有效地识别对RAG生成真正有帮助的文档，相比单纯相关性优化更贴近最终生成目标，并具备训练免费、可插拔和跨模型泛化的实用价值。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) depends on document ranking to provide useful evidence for generation, but conventional reranking methods mainly optimize query-document relevance rather than generation usefulness. A relevant document may still introduce noise, while a lower-ranked document may better reduce the generator's uncertainty. We propose CAR (Confidence-Aware Reranking), a query-guided, training-free, and plug-and-play reranking framework that uses generator confidence change as a document usefulness signal. CAR estimates confidence through the semantic consistency of multiple sampled answers under query-only and query-document conditions. Documents that significantly increase confidence are promoted, those that decrease confidence are demoted, and uncertain cases preserve the baseline order, while a query-level gate avoids unnecessary intervention on already confident queries. Experiments on four BEIR datasets show that CAR consistently improves NDCG@5 across sparse and dense retrievers, LLM-based and supervised rerankers, and four LLM backbones. Notably, CAR improves the YesNo reranker by 25.4 percent on average under Contriever retrieval, and its ranking gains strongly correlate with downstream generation F1 improvements, achieving Spearman rho = 0.964.

### [91] [SCOUT: Active Information Foraging for Long-Text Understanding with Decoupled Epistemic States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04496)
*Zhenliang Zhang,Wenqing Wang,Yong Hu,Yaming Yang,Jiaheng Gao,Chen Shen,Xiaojun Wan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 SCOUT，一种面向百万 token 长文本理解的主动信息搜寻范式，在保持推理可靠性的同时显著降低 token 消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 百万级长文本理解需要兼顾推理保真度与计算效率。现有长上下文大模型可端到端处理超长文本，但成本高且存在注意力稀释；专用 LTU agent 又常因图构建、索引等任务无关抽象损失关键信息。作者观察到：与查询相关的信息通常只占全文很小一部分，因此应围绕查询充分的子集进行推理。

Method: 提出 SCOUT，将文档视为可探索环境，从被动处理全文转向主动信息觅食。系统维护一个紧凑且带来源依据的认知状态，通过状态级缺口诊断引导，在粗到细探索与锚定式状态更新之间自适应切换，逐步收缩认知状态，使其达到对查询足够的信息覆盖。

Result: 实验表明，SCOUT 能匹配最先进专有模型的表现，同时最多减少 8 倍 token 消耗；并且在上下文长度扩展时表现稳定。

Conclusion: SCOUT 证明了基于查询充分子集的主动探索机制可以有效缓解长文本理解中的成本—性能权衡，在百万 token 场景下兼具效率、稳定性和推理保真度。

Abstract: Long-Text Understanding (LTU) at million-token scale requires balancing reasoning fidelity with computational efficiency. Frontier long-context LLMs can process millions of token contexts end-to-end, but they suffer from high token consumption and attention dilution. In parallel, specialized LTU agents often sacrifice fidelity through task-agnostic abstractions like graph construction or indexing. We identify a key insight for LTU: query-relevant information is typically sparse relative to the full document, so effective reasoning should rely on a query-sufficient subset rather than the entire context. To address this, we propose SCOUT, a new paradigm for LTU that shifts from passive processing to active information foraging. It treats the document as an explorable environment and answers from a compact, provenance-grounded epistemic state. Guided by state-level gap diagnosis, SCOUT adaptively alternates between coarse-to-fine exploration and anchored state updates that progressively contract its epistemic state toward query sufficiency. Experiments show that SCOUT matches state-of-the-art proprietary models while reducing token consumption by up to 8x. Moreover, SCOUT remains stable as context length scales, substantially alleviating the practical cost-performance trade-off.

### [92] [Distilling Bayesian Belief States into Language Models for Auditable Negotiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04507)
*Zongqi Cui,Baihan Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 BOND：一种用于可审计谈判的贝叶斯对手信念蒸馏框架，通过显式建模并输出对手偏好后验，提高谈判性能与信念校准可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谈判智能体需要在多轮对话中推断对手偏好并在不确定性下决策。端到端 LLM 虽能生成谈判对话，但其对手信念通常隐式存在，难以检查、校准和审计。

Method: BOND 包含两部分：一是基于 LLM 的贝叶斯教师模型，对六种可能的对手优先级排序进行打分并更新后验分布，用于菜单式决策；二是较小的 8B 学生语言模型，通过蒸馏学习同时输出谈判动作和归一化的后验信念标签文本。论文还使用后验轨迹、信念-策略误差分解和后验前缀干预进行诊断分析。

Result: 在 CaSiNo 谈判数据集上，BOND 超越已有最优方法；教师模型对对手优先级后验的平均 Brier 分数为 0.085。蒸馏后的 8B 学生模型保留了较多信念信号，Brier 分数为 0.114，优于六种排序均匀参考值 5/36（约 0.139）。与 70B structured-CoT 基线相比，8B 学生模型具有更好的后验校准。

Conclusion: BOND 证明了显式贝叶斯信念建模与蒸馏可提升谈判智能体的可审计性和校准能力；但诊断结果也显示，蒸馏更强地保留了可评分的信念报告，而非真正因果驱动的信念条件控制，从而暴露了信念与动作之间耦合不足的问题。

Abstract: Negotiation agents must infer what their counterpart values, update those beliefs over dialogue turns, and choose actions under uncertainty. End-to-end large language models (LLMs) can imitate negotiation dialogue, but their opponent beliefs are usually implicit and difficult to inspect. We propose BOND (Bayesian Opponent-belief Negotiation Distillation), a framework for auditable negotiation. BOND consists of an LLM-based Bayesian teacher that scores dialogue contexts against the six possible opponent priority orderings, updates a posterior over those orderings, and uses the posterior for menu-based decision making, as well as a smaller 8B student language model that emits both negotiation actions and normalized posterior beliefs as tagged text. In the CaSiNo negotiation dataset, BOND outperforms the state-of-the-art and achieves mean Brier score 0.085 over opponent-priority posteriors. The distilled student preserves much of this belief signal, achieving Brier 0.114, below the uniform six-ordering reference of 5/36, approximately 0.139. Compared with a 70B structured-CoT baseline, the significantly smaller 8B student model yields substantially better elicited posterior calibration. We further showcase auditability through posterior trajectories, belief-versus-policy error decomposition, and posterior-prefix interventions. These diagnostics reveal that distillation preserves a scoreable belief report more strongly than causal belief-conditioned control, making weak belief-action coupling visible, not hidden.

</details>

Ablations show that diversity in model families, scales, and prompting strategies is essential, with the ensemble consistently beating any single model. We also introduce Meno-Lite-0.1, a 7B domain-adapted model with a strong cost--performance trade-off, and analyse MTRAGEval, highlighting annotation limitations and directions for improvement.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 DPO/RLHF 偏好信号常偏向流畅、冗长回答，而非逻辑正确性，导致知识密集型任务中 SFT 模型虽语言流畅但 NLI 蕴含分数很低，存在逻辑对齐缺口。

Method: 构建 Hybrid-DPO 自动偏好管线，融合 DeBERTa-v3 的 NLI 信号与 verifier LLM 评分，替代人工标注或单一 LLM judge 偏好信号，并在多学科、多模型架构上进行评估。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), the efficient alternative to PPO-based RLHF, falls short on knowledge-intensive generation: standard preference signals from human annotators or LLM judges exhibit a systematic verbosity bias that rewards fluency over logical correctness. We propose RLearner-LLM with Hybrid-DPO: an automated preference pipeline that fuses a DeBERTa-v3 NLI signal with a verifier LLM score, removing human annotation while overcoming the "alignment tax" of single-signal optimization. On Gemma 4 E4B-it (4.5B effective params), Hybrid-DPO lifts NLI in four of five domains (+11.9% to +2.4x) with faster inference across all five, scaling down to compact base models without losing the alignment-tax mitigation. Our Qwen3-8B RLearner-LLM wins 95% of pairwise comparisons against its own SFT baseline; GPT-4o-mini in turn wins 95% against our concise output -- alongside the 69% win the same judge gives a verbose SFT over our DPO model, this replicates verbosity bias on a frontier comparator and motivates logic-aware metrics (NLI, ACR) over LLM-as-a-judge for knowledge-intensive generation.

### [95] [UniVer: A Unified Perspective for Multi-step and Multi-draft Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04543)
*Yepeng Weng,Qiao Hu,Takehisa Yairi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 UniVer，将树状 speculative decoding 验证统一建模为条件最优传输问题，联合优化多草稿与多步候选的接受过程，在保持目标模型分布精确一致的同时提升接受长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 speculative decoding 验证方法通常将多草稿分支与多步依赖分开处理：要么对单步草稿使用平坦 OT，要么对树状候选使用逐 token 拒绝采样。这种局部化处理无法充分利用候选树横向分支与纵向前缀依赖之间的耦合关系，导致联合场景下验证效率不足。

Method: 作者提出条件 OT 视角，将树状验证建模为带前缀约束的最优传输问题。核心做法是用前缀接受概率抽象纵向依赖，并将其作为动态缩放因子来指导横向草稿选择。在此基础上提出 UniVer，通过在前缀约束下组合局部最优传输计划，实现跨树层级的联合优化。

Result: 实验显示，在不同任务和模型上，UniVer 相比标准的无放回递归拒绝采样可将 acceptance length 提升 4.2% 到 8.5%，同时保持与目标模型完全一致的分布对齐。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，将树状 speculative decoding 验证统一为条件 OT 可以更有效地利用多步依赖与多草稿分支的耦合关系。UniVer 在理论上无损并达到条件框架下的最优接受率，实践中也带来稳定的解码效率提升。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates Large Language Models via draft-then-verify, where verification can be framed as an Optimal Transport (OT) problem. Existing approaches typically handle multi-draft and multi-step aspects in isolation, applying either flat OT to single-step drafts or per-token rejection sampling to tree-structured candidates. This separation leaves the joint regime (where multi-step dependencies meet multi-draft branching) poorly optimized, as local verification rules fail to exploit the coupling between horizontal and vertical dimensions of candidate trees. In this paper, we propose a unified perspective that casts tree-based verification as a conditional OT problem. Our key insight is that vertical dependencies can be abstracted through prefix acceptance probabilities, which act as dynamic scaling factors to actively guide horizontal draft selection. Based on this principle, we introduce UniVer, a verification algorithm that jointly optimizes across tree levels by composing local optimal transport plans under prefix constraints. We prove that UniVer remains lossless and achieves the optimal acceptance rate under the proposed conditional framework. Extensive experiments across different tasks and models demonstrate that UniVer improves acceptance length by 4.2% to 8.5% over standard recursive rejection sampling without replacement, while maintaining exact distributional alignment with the target model.
