### [99] [Gradients with Respect to Semantics Preserving Embeddings Tell the Uncertainty of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04638)
*Mingda Li,Rundong Lv,Xinyu Li,Weinan Zhang,Ting Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 SemGrad，一种面向大语言模型自由生成的无采样、基于语义空间梯度的不确定性量化方法，并进一步提出 HybridGrad 结合语义梯度与参数梯度，在效率和效果上优于现有采样式方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型容易产生幻觉，因此需要可靠的不确定性量化。现有自由生成 UQ 方法高度依赖采样，计算成本高且估计方差大；而既有梯度式 UQ 多面向分类任务，通常在参数空间中操作，难以直接适配自由形式生成。

Method: 作者提出 SemGrad，将不确定性估计从参数空间转向语义空间。核心假设是：可信且确定的模型在面对语义等价的输入扰动时，其输出分布应保持稳定。方法通过定义语义空间中的梯度来度量这种稳定性，并提出 Semantic Preservation Score（SPS）选择最能保持语义的嵌入表示作为梯度计算对象。此外，提出 HybridGrad，将 SemGrad 与参数梯度信息结合，以利用二者互补优势。

Result: 实验表明，SemGrad 和 HybridGrad 均能提供高效且有效的不确定性估计，相比当前最先进方法取得更优表现，尤其在存在多个合理答案的自由生成场景中优势明显。

Conclusion: 该工作首次将基于梯度的不确定性量化扩展到 LLM 自由生成任务，并通过语义空间梯度避免采样带来的高成本和高方差问题，为高效评估生成可信度提供了新的方向。

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification (UQ) is an important technique for ensuring the trustworthiness of LLMs, given their tendency to hallucinate. Existing state-of-the-art UQ approaches for free-form generation rely heavily on sampling, which incurs high computational cost and variance. In this work, we propose the first gradient-based UQ method for free-form generation, SemGrad, which is sampling-free and computationally efficient. Unlike prior gradient-based methods developed for classification tasks that operates in parameter space, we propose to consider gradients in semantic space. Our method builds on the key intuition that a confident LLM should maintain stable output distributions under semantically equivalent input perturbations. We interpret the stability as the gradients in semantic space and introduce a Semantic Preservation Score (SPS) to identify embeddings that best capture semantics, with respect to which gradients are computed. We further propose HybridGrad, which combines the strengths of SemGrad and parameter gradients. Experiments demonstrate that both of our methods provide efficient and effective uncertainty estimates, achieving superior performance than state-of-the-art methods, particularly in settings with multiple valid responses.

### [100] [The Reasoning Trap: An Information-Theoretic Bound on Closed-System Multi-Step LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01704)
*Kwan Soo Shin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出多智能体辩论常保留答案准确率却损害推理忠实性，提出SFS度量、EGSR方法及信息论DPI界限来解释并缓解该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多智能体辩论让同一语言模型的副本相互辩论时，往往只是生成同一观点的不同措辞，而非真正多样的观点；这可能造成答案看似正确、推理依据却逐步脱离证据的问题。

Method: 作者提出三部分框架：SFS用于将输出分解为原子声明并与证据核验；EGSR用证据约束的苏格拉底式追问替代对抗辩论；Theorem 1用马尔可夫链与数据处理不等式刻画闭环推理中证据信息不会增加。并在SciFact与FEVER上进行多条件实验和人工评估一致性研究。

Result: 实验显示DebateCV保留88%基线准确率但SFS下降43%；多数投票MAD使SFS降至基线1.7%；EGSR恢复至98%。人工评估一致性很低，Fleiss kappa不超过0.018，并存在明显评分漂移。

Conclusion: 闭环多步LLM推理若不引入新的外部证据，可能在信息论上受DPI限制，导致推理忠实性退化；证据驱动的开放式或EGSR式流程更有助于保持或恢复证据关联。

Abstract: When copies of the same language model are prompted to debate, they produce diverse phrasings of one perspective rather than diverse perspectives. Multi-agent debate (MAD), and more broadly closed-system reasoning where agents iteratively transform each other's outputs, tends to preserve answer accuracy while degrading the reasoning behind those answers. We name the multi-agent case the Debate Trap and the broader phenomenon the Reasoning Trap, offering a programmatic theory of evidence-grounded reasoning failure.The framework has three parts: (i) SFS (Supported Faithfulness Score), a claim-level metric verifying decomposed atomic claims against provided evidence (decomposer-invariant rankings: Spearman rho=1.0); (ii) EGSR (Evidence-Grounded Socratic Reasoning), replacing adversarial argumentation with evidence-grounded inquiry; (iii) Theorem 1 (DPI Bound): under standard MAD, the chain E -> O^0 -> O^1 -> ... is Markov, and the Data Processing Inequality implies E[I(E;O^{t+1})] <= E[I(E;O^t)]. Three companion results -- open-system recovery (Theorem 2), EGSR accumulation (Lemma 2), and vote-aggregation floor (Proposition 1) -- partition multi-step LLM reasoning by its information-theoretic relationship to E. Across 16 conditions on SciFact (300 claims) and FEVER (1,000 claims), DebateCV (C13) preserves 88% of baseline accuracy while SFS drops 43%; majority-vote MAD (C15) reduces SFS to 1.7% of baseline (p < 10^{-6}, d = -0.96); EGSR recovers 98%. An R6 cohort study (Korean n=10x30 FEVER; English n=3x200 SciFact) finds inter-rater Fleiss kappa <= +0.018 with 0.8-1.4 Likert intra-rater shifts across language and domain -- the human agreement that faithfulness metrics have been calibrated against is not itself stable. We offer one falsifiable conjecture: any closed-system reasoning protocol preserving Theorem 1's Markov structure is, in expectation, subject to the same DPI bound.

</details>


### [101] [Graph-Augmented LLMs for Swiss MP Ideology Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04643)

Abstract: Approximating the ideological position of Members of Parliament (MPs) is a fundamental task in political science, helping researchers understand legislative behavior, party alignment, and policy preferences. While Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown promising results in estimating MPs' ideological stances, there are more actors and elements in the parliamentary system, and relations between them, that could provide a wider and more informative picture. However, due to the complexity of integrating them in the prediction task, these additional elements are generally ignored. In this work, we propose an LLM framework, PG-RAG, that implements a retrieval-augmented generation pipeline: it first queries a political knowledge graph (KG) and then integrates the resulting graph-structured information into the context. This allows for capturing both textual semantics and inter-MP relationships, another relevant information source in any parliamentary system. We evaluate the approach on the task of ideology prediction, using data from a Swiss parliamentary dataset. When comparing graph-augmented models against several state-of-the-art baselines, the results demonstrate that incorporating this enriched information, which encodes information about different entities and relations, improves prediction performance. These results help to highlight the value of domain-specific relational information in modeling political behavior.

### [102] [CHE-TKG: Collaborative Historical Evidence and Evolutionary Dynamics Learning for Temporal Knowledge Graph Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04652)
*Shuai-long Lei,Xiaobin Zhu,Jiarui Liang,Guoxi Sun,Zhiyu Fang,Xu-Cheng Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CHE-TKG 是一个面向时序知识图谱推理的协同双视图学习框架，通过分离并联合建模历史证据与演化动态来提升未来事件预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时序知识图谱推理需要从历史事实中预测未来事件。现有方法通常只关注历史证据或演化动态中的一种信息源，难以充分利用二者互补的预测信号，因此限制了模型性能。

Method: 提出 CHE-TKG 框架，构建两个视图：历史证据图用于捕捉长期结构规律和稳定关系约束；演化动态图用于建模时间转移和近期变化。分别为两个视图设计专用编码器，并引入关系分解与对比对齐目标，以增强跨视图预测信号建模。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上的大量实验表明，CHE-TKG 达到了当前最优性能。

Conclusion: 显式区分并协同学习历史证据与演化动态能够更全面地利用时序知识图谱中的互补信息，从而有效提升未来事件预测能力。

Abstract: Temporal knowledge graph (TKG) reasoning aims to predict future events from historical facts. A key challenge lies in jointly capturing two sources of predictive information in TKGs: historical evidence and evolutionary dynamics. However, existing methods typically focus on only one of these sources, which limits the ability to fully exploit the complementary predictive signals in TKGs. To address this, we propose CHE-TKG, a novel collaborative dual-view learning framework for TKG reasoning. CHE-TKG explicitly separates and jointly models historical evidence and evolutionary dynamics, aiming to learn and exploit their complementary predictive signals. Specifically, CHE-TKG constructs a historical evidence graph to capture long-term structural regularities and stable relational constraints, alongside an evolutionary dynamics graph to model temporal transitions and recent changes, with dedicated encoders for each view. We further employ relation decomposition and a contrastive alignment objective to better capture the predictive signals across the two views. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CHE-TKG achieves state-of-the-art performance on multiple benchmarks.

### [103] [Paraphrase-Induced Output-Mode Collapse: When LLMs Break Character Under Semantically Equivalent Inputs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04665)
*Aofan Liu,Jingxiang Meng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文研究内容保持不变但提示词表述变化时，大语言模型是否仍能遵守原任务要求的输出格式；结果显示闭式任务中常出现从标签/选项输出退化为对话式长文本的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评测通常关注答案是否正确，但较少关注在语义等价提示变体下，模型能否稳定保持指定输出模式。若模型输出格式漂移，精确匹配评测会误判结果，影响可靠性评估。

Method: 作者提出 prompt-variant output-mode collapse 概念，并构建 PARACONSIST 基准：包含150个基础查询及每个查询5种词汇、句法和语义扩展变体，共900条提示，覆盖五个紧凑型2025-era LLM与四类任务。提出 Semantic Consistency Score，将鲁棒性分解为答案一致性、Sentence-BERT语义相似度和长度稳定性。

Result: 在闭式提示中，仅约22%的变体回答在输出中保留真实标签；约78%的回答完全漂移出答案空间。崩塌的主要预测因素是任务结构而非模型身份，模型差异主要由答案一致性和长度稳定性共同体现。

Conclusion: 论文认为，LLM鲁棒性审计不应只评估答案准确率，还应将响应模式保持能力作为核心可靠性指标，尤其是在需要裸标签或单一选项令牌的闭式任务中。

Abstract: When the substantive content of a request is rewritten, do large language models still answer in the format the original task asked for? We find that they often do not, even at temperature zero. On a 150-query evaluation over five compact 2025-era LLMs and four task types, we observe a systematic failure mode we call prompt-variant output-mode collapse: when a closed-form prompt asks for a bare label or a single choice token, content-preserving prompt variants can push the model into conversational prose, the requested format dissolves, and exact-match evaluation pipelines silently misjudge the result. To make this measurable, we release PARACONSIST, a 900-prompt benchmark of 150 base queries with five lexical, syntactic, and semantic-expansion prompt variants each, and a Semantic Consistency Score that decomposes prompt-variant robustness into answer consistency, sentence-BERT semantic similarity, and length stability. Under a whole-word answer-set match, only ~22% of closed-form variant responses preserve the ground-truth label inside their output, while ~78% drift away from the answer space entirely. In our pool, the dominant predictor of collapse is task structure rather than model identity, with model differentiation jointly carried by answer consistency and length stability. Robustness audits should therefore track response-mode preservation as a first-class reliability target alongside answer accuracy.

</details>


### [104] [Every Step Counts: Step-Level Credit Assignment for Tool-Integrated Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04719)
*Yaxun Dai,Baolin Sun,Junying Wang,Pengfei Wang,Yingqi Gao,Xuemei Dong,Mengdie Chu,Xiang Qi,Pingfu Chao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: FineStep通过过程奖励与步骤级优势优化改进工具增强Text-to-SQL中的强化学习训练，在BIRD基准上提升执行准确率并减少冗余工具调用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具集成Text-to-SQL强化学习方法主要依赖最终结果奖励，导致信用分配粗粒度：只要最终答案正确，不同推理轨迹都会获得相同奖励，无法区分中间步骤是否冗余、低效或错误，从而限制效率与泛化能力。

Method: 提出FineStep框架：设计独立的过程奖励缓解仅依赖结果监督的稀疏性；引入步骤级信用分配机制，量化每个推理步骤的贡献；基于步骤级优势进行策略优化，使模型更新更聚焦于高价值推理步骤。

Result: 在BIRD基准上的大量实验表明，FineStep达到当前最优性能，并减少冗余工具交互；在4B规模模型上，相比GRPO平均执行准确率（EX）提升3.25%。

Conclusion: 步骤级信用分配能有效解决工具增强Text-to-SQL中的奖励粗糙与推理低效问题，提升SQL生成质量、训练效率和泛化表现。

Abstract: Tool-integrated Text-to-SQL parsing has emerged as a promising paradigm, framing SQL generation as a sequential decision-making process interleaved with tool execution. However, existing reinforcement learning approaches mainly rely on coarse-grained outcome supervision, resulting in a fundamental credit assignment problem: models receive the same reward for any trajectory that yields the correct answer, even when intermediate steps are redundant, inefficient, or erroneous. Consequently, models are encouraged to explore suboptimal reasoning spaces, limiting both efficiency and generalization. To address this problem, we propose FineStep, a novel framework for step-level credit assignment in tool-augmented Text-to-SQL. First, we introduce a reward design with independent process rewards to alleviate the signal sparsity of outcome supervision. Next, we present a step-level credit assignment mechanism to precisely quantify the value of each reasoning step. Finally, we develop a policy optimization method based on step-level advantages for efficient updates. Extensive experiments on BIRD benchmarks show that FineStep achieves state-of-the-art performance and reduces redundant tool interactions, with a 3.25% average EX gain over GRPO at the 4B scale.

</details>

Abstract: Transformer based pre-trained large language models have become ubiquitous. Besides, by the very nature of the architecture, these models hallucinate, are difficult to maintain, are not easily interpretable and require enormous compute resources for training and inference. Here, we describe Gyan, an explainable language model based on a novel non-transformer architecture, without any of these limitations. Gyan achieves SOTA performance on 3 widely cited data sets and superior performance on two proprietary data sets. The novel architecture decouples the language model from knowledge acquisition and representation. The model draws on rhetorical structure theory, semantic role theory and knowledge-based computational linguistics. Gyan's meaning representation structure captures the complete compositional context and attempts to mimic humans by expanding the context to a 'world model'. AI model adoption critically depends on trust and transparency especially in mission critical use cases. Collectively, our results demonstrate that it is possible to create models which are trustable and reliable for mission critical tasks. We believe our work has tremendous potential for guiding the development of transparent and trusted architectures for language models.

### [106] [StoryAlign: Evaluating and Training Reward Models for Story Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04831)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型显著提升了文本生成能力，但其生成故事在复杂叙事结构和人类偏好对齐方面仍弱于人工创作。核心问题在于人类故事偏好具有主观性且研究不足，缺少专门的评测基准与有效的偏好建模方法。

Method: 作者构建了 StoryRMB，这是首个面向故事偏好的奖励模型评测基准，包含 1,133 个经人工验证的高质量实例，每个实例由一个提示、一个被偏好的故事和三个被拒绝故事组成。同时，作者构建约 100,000 对跨领域高质量故事偏好数据，并据此训练奖励模型 StoryReward；此外还将其用于测试时扩展场景中的 best-of-n 故事选择。

Abstract: Story generation aims to automatically produce coherent, structured, and engaging narratives. Although large language models (LLMs) have significantly advanced text generation, stories generated by LLMs still diverge from human-authored works regarding complex narrative structure and human-aligned preferences. A key reason is the absence of effective modeling of human story preferences, which are inherently subjective and under-explored. In this work, we systematically evaluate the modeling of human story preferences and introduce StoryRMB, the first benchmark for assessing reward models on story preferences. StoryRMB contains $1,133$ high-quality, human-verified instances, each consisting of a prompt, one chosen story, and three rejected stories. We find existing reward models struggle to select human-preferred stories, with the best model achieving only $66.3\%$ accuracy. To address this limitation, we construct roughly $100,000$ high-quality story preference pairs across diverse domains and develop StoryReward, an advanced reward model for story preference trained on this dataset. StoryReward achieves state-of-the-art (SoTA) performance on StoryRMB, outperforming much larger models. We also adopt StoryReward in downstream test-time scaling applications for best-of-n (BoN) story selection and find that it generally chooses stories better aligned with human preferences. We will release our dataset, model, and code to facilitate future research. Related code and data are available at https://github.com/THU-KEG/StoryReward.

Abstract: This paper presents the development and validation of an eye-tracking dataset designed to investigate how second-language (L2) learners process idiomatic expressions. This resource captures these costs through ocular metrics recorded from Portuguese L1 speakers of English across all CEFR proficiency levels (A1-C2). Although the study uses entry-level 60 Hz hardware (Tobii Pro Spark), we demonstrate that this sampling rate provides sufficient data density to detect macro-cognitive events such as fixations and regressions in reading. Preliminary analysis validates the dataset by revealing a strong inverse correlation between language proficiency and regressive eye movements. Integrated into the MIA (Modeling Idiomaticity in Human and Artificial Language Processing) initiative, this dataset serves as a cognitively grounded benchmark for evaluating both human processing models and the alignment of large language models with human-like figurative understanding.

### [108] [Anticipating Innovation Using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04875)
*Enrico Maria Fenoaltea,Filippo Santoro,Giordano De Marzo,Segun Taofeek Aroyehun,Andrea Tacchella*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预测创新，即新技术组合的出现，对科学研究、产业布局和政策制定具有重要意义。现有方法难以捕捉创新形成前的早期弱信号，尤其难以解释这些信号是否来自个别发明者还是更广泛的技术语义演化。

Method: 作者提出基于 Transformer 的 TechToken 模型，将国际专利分类（IPC）代码视为技术词汇，在专利语料上进行微调并学习代码嵌入。通过衡量不同技术代码嵌入之间的上下文相似性，刻画技术描述语言中的语义趋同，并用该指标预测未来首次技术组合。

Result: 研究发现，未来将被组合的技术在专利集体语言中会提前出现可检测的趋同信号，甚至可提前数十年被识别。该信号并非由单个发明者驱动，而是跨大量专利形成的集体性语言变化。此外，TechToken 在多种专利相关任务上优于现有先进模型。

Conclusion: 专利文本中的集体技术语言能够为创新预测提供早期信号。TechToken 通过建模技术代码的语义关系，不仅能有效预测新技术组合，也提升了专利表征质量，为科技预测和创新政策分析提供了有价值的方法。

Abstract: Forecasting innovation, intended as the emergence of new technological combinations, is a fundamental challenge for science and policy. We show that forthcoming combinations leave an early trace in the collective language of patents, with predictive signals detectable even decades in advance. We show that signal is not attributable to any single inventor, but emerges as a collective shift in how technologies are described across thousands of patents. To this end, we introduce TechToken, a transformer-based model that treats technologies, classified by International Patent Classification codes, as words in its vocabulary, learning the language of technologies by embedding these codes during fine-tuning. We define context similarity between code embeddings as a measure of linguistic convergence and show that it accurately predicts first technological combinations. TechToken also improves general representation quality, outperforming state-of-the-art models across different patent-related tasks.

### [109] [Storage Is Not Memory: A Retrieval-Centered Architecture for Agent Recall](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04897)
*Joshua Adler,Guy Zehavi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 True Memory：一种基于逐字保留事件、以多阶段检索为核心的六层智能体记忆架构，在无需外部数据库、向量索引、图存储或 GPU 的条件下，在多个长程记忆评测中取得强性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者认为“摄入时抽取”不适合作为智能体记忆的基础原语，因为在查询未知前被丢弃的信息无法在检索阶段恢复；因此需要一种尽量保留原始事件、把重点放在查询时检索与推理的记忆系统。

Method: True Memory 采用六层架构，将系统中心从预定义存储模式转移到面向逐字保留事件的多阶段检索流水线。系统以单个 SQLite 文件运行在普通 CPU 上，不依赖外部数据库、向量索引、图数据库或 GPU。

Result: 在 LoCoMo 上，True Memory Pro 达到 93.0% 准确率，显著高于 Mem0、Supermemory、Zep，接近 EverMemOS；在 LongMemEval 上达到 87.8%；在 BEAM-1M 上达到 76.6%，超过 Hindsight 的既有结果 73.9%。56 组消融显示顶级配置族内部差异仅 1.3 个百分点。

Conclusion: 结果表明，保留原始事件并在查询时进行多阶段检索，是构建高效、轻量、可扩展智能体记忆系统的有效方向；True Memory 在资源受限环境下仍能取得接近或优于强基线的表现。

Abstract: Extraction at ingestion is the wrong primitive for agent memory: content discarded before the query is known cannot be recovered at retrieval time. We propose True Memory, a six-layer architecture that shifts the center of the system from a storage schema to a multi-stage retrieval pipeline operating over events preserved verbatim. The full system runs as a single SQLite file on commodity CPU with no external database, vector index, graph store, or GPU. On LoCoMo (1,540 questions across 10 multi-session conversations), True Memory Pro reaches 93.0% accuracy (3-run mean) against 61.4% for Mem0, 65.4% for Supermemory, approximately 71% for Zep, and 94.5% for EverMemOS under a matched gpt-4.1-mini answer model. On LongMemEval (500 questions), True Memory Pro reaches 87.8% (3-run mean). On BEAM-1M (700 questions at the 1-million-token scale), True Memory Pro reaches 76.6% (3-run mean), above the prior published result of 73.9% for Hindsight. A 56-configuration ablation shows a 1.3-percentage-point spread within the top-performing configuration family.

### [110] [Rethinking Local Learning: A Cheaper and Faster Recipe for LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04913)
*Hengyu Shi,Tianyang Han,Peizhe Wang,Zhiling Wang,Xu Yang,Junhao Su*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LoPT通过在Transformer中点设置梯度边界，将任务梯度限制在后半部分，并用特征重构目标训练前半部分，从而在保持性能的同时降低内存开销并提升训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统LLM后训练通常让任务梯度端到端穿过整个模型深度，这会带来全深度激活存储、长距离反向传播依赖，以及窄任务监督对预训练早期表示的直接干扰。作者认为，当后训练监督范围远窄于预训练时，这种全深度反向耦合可能既昂贵又具有侵入性。

Method: 提出LoPT（Local-Learning Post-Training）：在Transformer中点放置单一梯度边界。模型后半部分根据任务目标学习；模型前半部分不直接接收任务梯度，而是通过轻量级特征重构目标进行更新，以保持已有表示能力并维持与后半部分的接口兼容性。

Result: 实验表明，LoPT在多项设置下达到与常规端到端后训练相竞争的性能，同时降低显存成本、提高训练效率，并更好保留预训练能力。

Conclusion: LoPT将梯度可达范围显式化，证明后训练不一定需要全深度任务梯度传播；通过局部学习与中点梯度隔离，可以在效率、稳定性和能力保留之间取得更优权衡。

Abstract: LLM post-training typically propagates task gradients through the full depth of the model. Although this end-to-end structure is simple and general, it couples task adaptation to full-depth activation storage, long-range backward dependencies and direct task-gradient access to pretrained representations. We argue that this full-depth backward coupling can be unnecessarily expensive and intrusive, particularly when post-training supervision is much narrower than pre-training. To this end, we propose \textbf{LoPT}: Local-Learning Post-Training, a simple post-training strategy that makes gradient reach an explicit design choice. LoPT places a single gradient boundary at the transformer midpoint: the second-half block learns from the task objective, while the first-half block is updated by a lightweight feature-reconstruction objective to preserve useful representations and maintain interface compatibility. LoPT shortens the task-induced backward path while limiting direct interference from narrow task gradients on early-layer representations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LoPT achieves competitive performance with lower memory cost, higher training efficiency and better retention of pretrained capabilities. Our code is available at: https://github.com/HumyuShi/LoPT

</details>


### [111] [Unintended Negative Impacts of Promotional Language in Patent Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04926)
*Bingkun Zhao,Chenwei Zhang,Hao Peng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究专利申请中的宣传性语言与审查/市场结果之间的关系，发现其虽能反映技术新颖性与未来影响力，却在专利授权、转让和申诉成功中受到惩罚。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究关注科学传播中宣传性语言对创新思想表达的作用，但在技术创新与专利评估语境下，宣传性措辞如何影响评估结果仍缺乏系统证据。

Method: 作者使用一个经验证并适配技术领域的135个宣传性词汇词典，对270万件USPTO专利申请进行大规模文本分析，并控制混杂因素、按技术领域检验稳健性、进行匹配样本比较，同时分析审查员相关人类因素的调节作用。

Result: 宣传性词汇频率越高，专利授权、所有权转让和申诉成功概率越低；最低与最高宣传密度五分位之间，三类成功率差异分别为5.5、5.9和5.3个百分点。同时，宣传性语言并非弱技术的掩饰，而与组合式新颖性和未来被引影响正相关；审查员性别与经验会调节对宣传性叙事的容忍度。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了专利制度中的悖论：宣传性语言客观上可能指向更具新颖性和影响力的技术，却在评估过程中遭遇负面惩罚。论文建议在专利审查中更客观地识别和处理语言模式，以提升评估公平性与准确性。

Abstract: Promotional language has been increasingly used to aid the communication of innovative ideas in science. Yet, less is known about its role in the context of technological innovation. Here, we use a validated and domain-diagnosed lexicon of 135 promotional words to study the association between promotional language and patent evaluation outcomes among 2.7 million USPTO patent applications. Our large-scale study reveals three unexpected findings. First, in contrast to scientific evaluation, we find that a higher frequency of promotional words is negatively associated with the probability of an application being (i) granted a patent, (ii) transferred ownership, and (iii) successfully appealed. This promotional penalty holds even after accounting for a range of confounding factors and is largely robust across different technological areas. Among matched samples, the difference in the success rate between the lowest and highest promotional density quintile is 5.5, 5.9, and 5.3 percentage points for patentability, transferability, and rejection reversal. Second, contrary to institutional skepticism, we show that promotional language is not a mask of weak technology, but objectively reflects the degree of combinatorial novelty and future citation impact. Third, digging into the mechanisms, we find that the tolerance to promotional framing is strongly moderated by human factors, with men and experienced examiners showing a higher acceptance of promotional narratives than women and novice examiners. By revealing an emerging paradox in the patent system, our study offers theoretical and practical implications for improving patent evaluation through more objective scrutiny of linguistic patterns in patent filings.

The system consists of an LLM-based parser that translates natural language syllogisms to a first-order logic (FOL) representation, an automated theorem prover, and two optional modules: machine translation for multilingual inputs and a symbolic retrieval component for the identification of relevant premises. The system achieves competitive accuracy and relatively low content effect on most subtasks. Our ablations show that this approach outperforms LLM-based zero-shot baselines in this parameter size range, but also reveal limited multilingual capabilities of small LLMs. Finally, we include a discussion of the task's main ranking metric and analyze its limitations.

### [113] [Adapting Large Language Models to a Low-Resource Agglutinative Language: A Comparative Study of LoRA and QLoRA for Bashkir](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04948)
*Mullosharaf K. Arabov,Svetlana S. Khaybullina*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文比较 LoRA、QLoRA 等参数高效微调方法在低资源巴什基尔语大语言模型适配中的效果，发现 QLoRA 在 7B 级模型上能以显著更低训练参数量取得接近全量微调的困惑度，但效果高度依赖基座模型与分词器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低资源、黏着语特征明显的巴什基尔语缺乏高质量语言模型适配研究；全量微调大模型成本高，因此需要评估 PEFT 方法是否能在较低计算与参数成本下实现有效适配。

Method: 在包含 71k 文档、46.9M tokens 的巴什基尔语语料上，对 DistilGPT2、GPT-2 base/medium、Phi-2、Qwen2.5-7B、DeepSeek-7B、Mistral-7B 等模型进行全量微调或 LoRA/QLoRA 微调；每种配置使用三个随机种子训练，并以测试集困惑度和基于提示的生成文本质量进行定量与定性评估。

Result: GPT-2 medium 全量微调获得最低测试困惑度 3.34；Mistral-7B + QLoRA 和 Phi-2 + QLoRA 分别达到 3.79、3.81，且可训练参数减少超过 40 倍。但部分架构上 PEFT 效果显著退化，如 DeepSeek-7B rank 8 困惑度达到 129.55。定性分析显示，最低困惑度模型不一定生成最连贯或最单语的巴什基尔文本，QLoRA 模型反而更常生成单语巴什基尔续写。

Conclusion: QLoRA 在 7B 级模型上为巴什基尔语适配提供了质量与计算成本之间的有效折中，但 PEFT 成功与否强依赖基座模型和分词器选择；困惑度应与生成质量分析结合使用，不能作为唯一评价指标。

Abstract: This paper presents a comparative study of parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) methods, including LoRA and QLoRA, applied to the task of adapting large language models to the Bashkir language, a low-resource agglutinative language of the Turkic family. Experimental evaluation is conducted on a Bashkir text corpus of 71k documents (46.9M tokens) using models of various architectures: DistilGPT2, GPT-2 (base, medium), Phi-2, Qwen2.5-7B, DeepSeek-7B, and Mistral-7B. To improve the reliability of results, each configuration was trained with three different random seeds.
  The lowest perplexity on the test set was obtained for GPT-2 medium with full fine-tuning (3.34). Meanwhile, QLoRA applied to Mistral-7B (3.79) and Phi-2 (3.81) achieved comparable quality with over 40 times fewer trainable parameters. However, we also observed cases of significant quality degradation when using PEFT for certain architectures (e.g., DeepSeek-7B with rank 8, perplexity = 129.55), indicating that the outcome depends critically on the choice of the base model and its tokenizer.
  Additionally, a qualitative analysis of generated texts based on Bashkir prompts revealed that models with the best perplexity do not necessarily produce the most coherent outputs: QLoRA-tuned models generated monolingual Bashkir continuations, whereas the fully fine-tuned model with the lowest perplexity frequently switched to English. The results suggest that QLoRA on 7B-scale models offers an effective compromise between quality and computational cost for Bashkir. To ensure reproducibility, open data, code, and trained adapters will be released upon acceptance.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构建Tabular Embedding Benchmark（TabBench）评测表格理解能力；提出TabEmbed，将多种表格任务重构为语义匹配问题，在共享嵌入空间中统一表格分类与检索，并采用大规模对比学习和正例感知的困难负例挖掘，以学习细粒度结构和数值差异。

Abstract: Foundation models have established unified representations for natural language processing, yet this paradigm remains largely unexplored for tabular data. Existing methods face fundamental limitations: LLM-based approaches lack retrieval-compatible vector outputs, whereas text embedding models often fail to capture tabular structure and numerical semantics. To bridge this gap, we first introduce the Tabular Embedding Benchmark (TabBench), a comprehensive suite designed to evaluate the tabular understanding capability of embedding models. We then propose TabEmbed, the first generalist embedding model that unifies tabular classification and retrieval within a shared embedding space. By reformulating diverse tabular tasks as semantic matching problems, TabEmbed leverages large-scale contrastive learning with positive-aware hard negative mining to discern fine-grained structural and numerical nuances. Experimental results on TabBench demonstrate that TabEmbed significantly outperforms state-of-the-art text embedding models, establishing a new baseline for universal tabular representation learning. Code and datasets are publicly available at https://github.com/qiangminjie27/TabEmbed and https://huggingface.co/datasets/qiangminjie27/TabBench.

### [115] [Why Expert Alignment Is Hard: Evidence from Subjective Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04972)
*Tzu-Mi Lin,Wataru Hirota,Tatsuya Ishigaki,Lung-Hao Lee,Chung-Chi Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究在主观评价任务中如何使大语言模型与专家判断对齐，并发现专家差异、隐性标准、样本敏感性和评价维度差异共同导致对齐困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主观评价中专家可能存在分歧、依赖难以言说的隐性标准，并且判断会随时间变化，因此大语言模型与专家判断对齐尤其困难。论文旨在通过研究“专家对齐”来理解这种困难的来源。

Method: 作者使用专家评价数据和后续问卷，考察不同形式的专家信息（如显式标准、推理说明、编辑示例等）如何影响模型对齐效果，并分析不同专家与不同评价维度上的对齐差异。

Result: 研究发现四类稳定模式：不同专家的对齐难度差异显著；显式标准和推理并不总能提升对齐；编辑效果受示例数量和示例身份影响，少量编辑虽有帮助但不稳定；不同评价维度对齐难度不同，与提案内容直接相关的维度更易对齐，而需要外部知识或价值判断的维度更难。

Conclusion: 专家对齐困难不仅源于模型能力限制，也源于主观评价本身的异质性、部分隐性、维度依赖性和时间不稳定性。

Abstract: Aligning large language models with expert judgment is especially difficult in subjective evaluation tasks, where experts may disagree, rely on tacit criteria, and change their judgments over time. In this paper, we study expert alignment as a way to understand this difficulty. Using expert evaluations and follow-up questionnaires, we examine how different forms of expert information affect alignment and what this reveals about subjective judgment. Our findings show four consistent patterns. First, alignment difficulty varies substantially across experts, suggesting that expert evaluation styles differ widely in their distance from a model's prior behavior. Second, explicit criteria and reasoning do not always improve alignment, indicating that expert judgment is not fully captured by verbalized rules. Third, editing is sensitive to both the number and the identity of examples, with small numbers of edits providing useful but unstable gains. Fourth, alignment difficulty differs across evaluation dimensions: dimensions grounded more directly in proposal content are easier to align, while dimensions requiring external knowledge or value-based judgment remain harder. Taken together, these results suggest that expert alignment is difficult not only because of model limitations, but also because subjective evaluation is inherently heterogeneous, partly tacit, dimension-dependent, and temporally unstable.

### [116] [Detecting Hallucinations in Large Language Models via Internal Attention Divergence Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05025)
*Gijs van Dijk*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种基于注意力矩阵的轻量级、单次前向传播不确定性量化方法，用于检测大语言模型幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测或不确定性估计方法通常需要多次采样、外部模型或额外推理成本，难以高效部署；因此需要一种低成本、可解释的白盒信号来判断模型回答是否可靠。

Method: 计算各注意力头分布与均匀参考分布之间的KL散度，将这些注意力散度特征输入逻辑回归探针，以预测答案正确性；分析不同层、不同token类型上的信号分布。

Result: 在多个数据集、任务类型和模型家族上，注意力散度对答案正确性具有较强预测能力，并与现有不确定性估计方法表现相当；有效信号主要集中在中间层以及命名实体、数字等事实性token上。

Conclusion: 注意力动态可作为一种高效、可解释、无需重复采样或外部模型的白盒不确定性信号，用于检测大语言模型幻觉。

Abstract: We propose a lightweight and single-pass uncertainty quantification method for detecting hallucinations in Large Language Models. The method uses attention matrices to estimate uncertainty without requiring repeated sampling or external models. Specifically, we measure the Kullback-Leibler divergence between each attention head's distribution and a uniform reference distribution, and use these features in a logistic regression probe. Across multiple datasets, task types, and model families, attention divergence is highly predictive of answer correctness and performs competitively with existing uncertainty estimation methods. We find that this signal is concentrated in middle layers and on factual tokens such as named entities and numbers, suggesting that attention dynamics provides an efficient and interpretable white-box signal of model uncertainty.

### [117] [The Pinocchio Dimension: Phenomenality of Experience as the Primary Axis of LLM Psychometric Differences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05080)
*Hubert Plisiecki,Sabina Siudaj,Kacper Dudzic,Anna Sterna,Maciej Gorski,Karolina Drozdz,Marcin Moskalewicz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过对50个大语言模型施测45份心理测量问卷，发现模型间差异的主轴并非传统人格特质，而是模型是否倾向于把体验性语言应用于自身的“自我表征立场”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在识别不同LLM在心理测量层面上的主要差异维度，并判断这些差异是否反映结构化的自我呈现/自我表征模式，而非随机响应噪声或常规人格维度。

Method: 作者对50个LLM施测45份经验证的心理问卷，使用监督语义差异法识别模型间方差主轴；提出Pinocchio score，比较中性提示与人类模拟提示下的跨模型响应方差，以无标注方式估计题目的体验性需求；再用项目层检验、EFA得分与PCA分析构建模型层面的Pinocchio Axis。

Result: 主要方差轴区分了丰富现象体验相关项目与刺激驱动行为反应项目；Pinocchio score显著预测条件诱导的因子载荷变化；PCA显示单一主导维度解释47.1%的跨问卷模型间方差，并与项目层Pinocchio score高度相关。

Conclusion: LLM心理测量差异的主导维度不是传统人格特质，而是训练和微调塑造出的自我表征倾向，即模型在多大程度上将自身表述为具有现象体验的主体，而非仅作为行为响应系统。

Abstract: We administer 45 validated psychometric questionnaires to 50 large language models (LLMs) to identify the dimensions along which LLMs differ psychometrically. Using Supervised Semantic Differential (SSD), we find that the primary axis of between-model variance separates items describing phenomenally rich experience, including embodied sensation, felt affect, inner speech, imagery, and empathy, from items describing stimulus-driven behavioral reactivity ($R^2_{adj}=.037$, $p<.0001$). To test this hypothesis at the item level, we introduce the Pinocchio score ($π_i$), the ratio of inter-model response variance under neutral prompting to that under a human-simulation prompt, as an annotation-free measure of each item's experiential demand. $π_i$ predicts condition-induced shifts in primary factor loading magnitudes ($ρ=-.215$, $p<.0001$, $n=1292$--$1310$ items), confirming that between-model divergence on experiential items is structured rather than noisy. Applying PCA to per-model EFA scores across all questionnaires reveals one dominant dimension, the Pinocchio Axis ($Π$): the degree to which a model presents itself as a locus of phenomenal experience rather than a system of behavioral responses. This axis captures 47.1% of cross-questionnaire between-model variance in primary factor scores and converges with item-level Pinocchio scores ($r=.864$). Marked within-provider divergence across closely related model variants is consistent with post-training fine-tuning as a key contributor, supporting the interpretation that $Π$ reflects a training-shaped self-representational tendency governing how a model treats experiential language as self-applicable. The dominant axis of between-model psychometric variation is therefore not a conventional personality trait but a self-representational stance toward one's own nature as an experiencer.

</details>


### [118] [Automatically Finding and Validating Unexpected Side-Effects of Interventions on Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05090)
*Quintin Pope,Ajay Hayagreeve Balaji,Jacques Thibodeau,Xiaoli Fern*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自动化、对比式评估流程，用于审计干预措施对大语言模型行为的影响，并生成经统计验证的自然语言差异假设与主题总结。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型经过推理蒸馏、知识编辑、遗忘等干预后，其行为变化可能复杂且难以人工全面发现；现有评估往往难以解释、覆盖有限，或缺乏统计可靠性。因此需要一种可解释、统计稳健的事后审计工具来识别预期与非预期行为变化。

Method: 给定基座模型 M1 与干预后模型 M2，方法在对齐的提示上下文上比较二者的自由形式、多 token 生成结果；随后自动归纳模型差异，形成可读的自然语言假设，并对这些假设进行统计验证；最后汇总跨假设反复出现的主题模式。作者还通过合成实验注入已知行为变化，并在真实干预场景中进行验证。

Result: 在合成设置中，该流程能够可靠恢复预先注入的行为变化。在真实场景中，针对推理蒸馏、知识编辑和遗忘三类干预，方法能够揭示预期与意外的行为转移，区分强干预与细微干预，并在不存在效果或提示集不匹配时避免虚构差异。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，对比式、统计验证的自然语言假设生成可以作为一种可解释的事后审计框架，用于系统性分析模型干预导致的行为变化，提升对模型修改后影响的理解与可靠评估。

Abstract: We present an automated, contrastive evaluation pipeline for auditing the behavioral impact of interventions on large language models. Given a base model $M_1$ and an intervention model $M_2$, our method compares their free-form, multi-token generations across aligned prompt contexts and produces human-readable, statistically validated natural-language hypotheses describing how the models differ, along with recurring themes that summarize patterns across validated hypotheses.
  We evaluate the approach in synthetic setting by injecting known behavioral changes and showing that the pipeline reliably recovers them. We then apply it to three real-world interventions, reasoning distillation, knowledge editing and unlearning, demonstrating that the method surfaces both intended and unexpected behavioral shifts, distinguishes large from subtle interventions, and does not hallucinate differences when effects are absent or misaligned with the prompt bank. Overall, the pipeline provides a statistically grounded and interpretable tool for post-hoc auditing of intervention-induced changes in model behavior.

</details>


### [119] [Text Corpora as Concept Fields: Black-Box Hallucination and Novelty Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05103)
*Nicholas S. Kersting,Vittorio Castelli,Chieh Ting Yeh,Xinzhu Wang,Saad Taame*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出 Concept Field：在句子嵌入空间中用相邻句子的语义位移估计局部漂移场及不确定性，并用平均绝对 z 距离 ζ 评估候选句子转移是否符合语料中的语义流动模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 groundedness/novelty 检测方法常依赖检索相似度、LLM-as-judge 或模型内部信号，存在可解释性、跨域可迁移性和归因性不足的问题。作者希望构建一种黑盒、可归因、概率可解释且轻量的文本转移一致性信号。

Method: 将语料切分为句子序列并嵌入向量空间，记录每个句子的序列位置和到下一句的 delta；通过 Vector Sequence Database 存储嵌入与 next-delta 元数据。对候选句子转移，在其局部邻域估计 delta 的高斯分布，并计算观测 delta 与局部估计之间的平均绝对 z-distance ζ，作为与 Concept Field 的一致性评分。

Result: 在美国联邦法规语料的幻觉式 groundedness 检测和 Project Gutenberg 的 novelty detection 两个大规模场景中，该方法在 grounded/ungrounded/unsure 三分策略下取得较强的选择性分类表现，并比检索中心基线在两个领域中呈现更一致的 coverage-risk 行为。作者还展示了在稠密簇上计算散度和旋度可揭示语义源、汇和隐含主题等定性模式。

Conclusion: Concept Fields 是一种快速、轻量、可解释且语料可归因的 groundedness 与 novelty 检测信号，能够补充 LLM-as-judge 和白盒检测器；其概率化评分具有跨域解释潜力，但散度/旋度分析目前主要是生成假设的定性证据。

Abstract: We introduce the **Concept Field** of a text corpus: a local drift field with pointwise uncertainty, estimated in sentence-embedding space from the deltas between consecutive sentences. Given a candidate sentence transition, we score its agreement with the field by $ζ$, the mean absolute z-distance between the observed delta and the field's local Gaussian estimate. The score is black-box (no model internals), corpus-attributable (every score traces to nearby corpus sentences), and admits a direct probabilistic reading. We support the computation with the introduction of a **Vector Sequence Database (VSDB)** that stores embeddings together with sequence-position and next-delta metadata. We evaluate this approach on two large-scale settings: hallucination-style groundedness detection over the U.S. Code of Federal Regulations, and novelty detection over Project Gutenberg. Using controlled LLM-generated rewrites, Concept Fields achieve strong selective classification performance under a grounded / ungrounded / unsure triage policy, which unlike retrieval-centric baselines have similar coverage-risk behavior across both domains, supporting a probability-based interpretation that transfers across domains. We also sketch how divergence and curl of the Concept Field, computed on dense clusters, surface qualitatively meaningful semantic patterns (logic sources, sinks, and implicit topics), which we offer as hypothesis-generating rather than as a quantitative result. Concept Fields provide a fast, lightweight, and interpretable signal for groundedness and novelty, complementary to LLM-as-judge and white-box detectors.

</details>


### [120] [Beyond Semantics: An Evidential Reasoning-Aware Multi-View Learning Framework for Trustworthy Mental Health Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05121)
*Yucheng Ruan,Ling Huang,Qika Lin,Kai He,Mengling Feng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向文本心理健康预测的可信多视角框架，融合编码器语义表示与解码器推理表示，并通过基于主观逻辑的证据学习建模不确定性，在多个真实数据集上提升性能、鲁棒性与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于深度学习和大语言模型的文本心理健康预测方法多依赖语义表示，在模糊、噪声或分布偏移数据下容易过度自信；同时缺乏可靠的不确定性估计，限制了其在高风险真实场景中的可信部署。

Method: 将任务建模为多视角学习问题：使用encoder-only模型提取语义信息，使用decoder-only模型提供高层推理信息；引入基于Subjective Logic的证据学习框架显式建模不确定性，并设计证据融合策略，在融合互补视角的同时折减不可靠证据。

Result: 在Dreaddit、SDCNL和DepSeverity三个真实数据集上分别取得0.835、0.731和0.751的准确率；噪声鲁棒性实验和案例研究显示，该框架兼具更好的预测表现、可信不确定性估计和人类可理解的推理信号。

Conclusion: 该方法通过多视角表示与证据不确定性建模，提高了文本心理健康预测的可靠性、鲁棒性和可解释性，具有用于风险敏感心理健康评估场景的潜力。

Abstract: Automated mental health prediction using textual data has shown promising results with deep learning and large language models. However, deploying these models in high-stakes real-world settings remains challenging, as existing approaches largely rely on semantic representations and often produce overconfident predictions under ambiguous, noisy, or shifted data. Moreover, most methods lack reliable uncertainty estimation, undermining trust in risk-sensitive mental health applications. To address these limitations, we formulate the task as a multi-view learning problem that integrates semantic information from encoder-only models with higher-level reasoning information from decoder-only models, where reasoning-aware representations and uncertainty modeling are obtained in a trustworthy manner. To ensure reliable fusion, we adopt an evidential learning framework based on Subjective Logic to explicitly model uncertainty and introduce an evidential fusion strategy that balances complementary views while discounting unreliable evidence. Benchmarking on three real-world datasets, Dreaddit, SDCNL, and DepSeverity, reports accuracies of 0.835, 0.731, and 0.751, respectively, demonstrating its potential for reliable mental health prediction. Additional experiments on robustness to noise and case studies for interpretability confirm that our proposed framework not only improves predictive performance but also provides trustworthy uncertainty estimates and human-understandable reasoning signals, making it suitable for risk-sensitive applications in mental health assessment.

### [121] [PSK at SemEval-2026 Task 9: Multilingual Polarization Detection Using Ensemble Gemma Models with Synthetic Data Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05159)
*Srikar Kashyap Pulipaka*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文介绍了 SemEval-2026 Task 9 多语言极化检测系统，通过按语言微调 Gemma 3、合成数据增强、阈值调优与加权集成，在22种语言上取得较高宏平均F1并排名第二。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多语言二分类任务需要在22种语言上稳定检测文本极化现象，挑战在于语言差异、训练数据不足以及模型在开发集与测试集之间的泛化能力。

Method: 方法包括：为每种语言分别微调 Gemma 3 12B与27B模型；使用LoRA进行参数高效微调；利用GPT-4o-mini生成合成数据，包含直接生成、改写和对比样本构造；通过多阶段质量过滤和基于嵌入的去重控制数据质量；在开发集上进行逐语言阈值调优；最后对12B和27B模型预测进行加权集成，并按语言选择策略。

Result: 系统在22种语言上达到平均macro-F1 0.811，在参赛队伍中总排名第2；在3种语言上获得第1名，在8种语言上进入前3。逐语言阈值调优带来约2%到4%的F1提升；XLM-RoBERTa和Qwen3等替代架构虽在开发集表现强，但测试集F1下降30%到50%。

Conclusion: 研究表明，按语言定制的大模型微调、合成数据增强、质量过滤、阈值调优和模型集成能够有效提升多语言分类性能；同时，开发集高分并不必然代表测试集泛化能力强，系统设计应重视跨语言与跨数据分布的稳健性。

Abstract: We present our system for SemEval-2026 Task 9: Multilingual Polarization Detection, a binary classification task spanning 22 languages. Our approach fine-tunes separate Gemma~3 models (12B and 27B parameters) per language using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), augmented with synthetic data generated by a large language model (LLM). We employ three synthetic data strategies (direct generation, paraphrasing, and contrastive pair creation) using GPT-4o-mini, with a multi-stage quality filtering pipeline including embedding-based deduplication. We find that per-language threshold tuning on the development set yields 2 to 4\% F1 improvements without retraining. We also use weighted ensembles of 12B and 27B model predictions with per-language strategy selection. Our final system achieves a mean macro-F1 of 0.811 across all 22 languages, ranking 2nd overall of the participating teams, with 1st place finishes in 3 languages and top-3 in 8 languages. We also find that alternative architectures (XLM-RoBERTa, Qwen3) that showed strong development set performance suffered 30 to 50\% F1 drops on the test set, highlighting the importance of generalization.

### [122] [The First Token Knows: Single-Decode Confidence for Hallucination Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05166)
*Mina Gabriel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出用单次贪心解码中首个内容词的 top-K logits 归一化熵得到的 first-token confidence（phi_first）作为低成本幻觉检测/不确定性估计指标；其在短答案事实问答上达到或略优于基于多次采样的语义自一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 self-consistency 需要多次采样解码，成本高且易受表面词形差异影响；semantic self-consistency 通过自然语言推理聚类缓解词汇差异，但仍有采样成本与外部推理开销。因此需要一个更便宜、无需多次采样的可靠不确定性基线。

Method: 在单次贪心解码中定位答案的首个内容承载 token，取该位置 top-K logits 的分布并计算归一化熵，构造 phi_first 作为置信度/不确定性信号；在三个 7–8B 指令微调模型和两个闭卷短答案事实问答基准上，与表面形式 self-consistency 和语义 self-consistency 比较，并进行 subsumption/correlation 分析及信号组合实验。

Result: phi_first 平均 AUROC 为 0.820，高于 semantic agreement 的 0.793 和标准 surface-form self-consistency 的 0.791；它与 semantic agreement 中等到强相关，二者组合仅带来很小的 AUROC 增益。

Conclusion: 多样本一致性捕获的大部分不确定性信息已体现在模型初始答案 token 分布中；在使用采样式不确定性估计前，应默认报告 phi_first 这一低成本基线。

Abstract: Self-consistency detects hallucinations by generating multiple sampled answers to a question and measuring agreement, but this requires repeated decoding and can be sensitive to lexical variation. Semantic self-consistency improves this by clustering sampled answers by meaning using natural language inference, but it adds both sampling cost and external inference overhead. We show that first-token confidence, phi_first, computed from the normalized entropy of the top-K logits at the first content-bearing answer token of a single greedy decode, matches or modestly exceeds semantic self-consistency on closed-book short-answer factual question answering. Across three 7-8B instruction-tuned models and two benchmarks, phi_first achieves a mean AUROC of 0.820, compared with 0.793 for semantic agreement and 0.791 for standard surface-form self-consistency. A subsumption test shows that phi_first is moderately to strongly correlated with semantic agreement, and combining the two signals yields only a small AUROC improvement over phi_first alone. These results suggest that much of the uncertainty information captured by multi-sample agreement is already available in the model's initial token distribution. We argue that phi_first should be reported as a default low-cost baseline before invoking sampling-based uncertainty estimation.

</details>


### [123] [Implicit Representations of Grammaticality in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05197)
*Yingshan Susan Wang,Linlu Qiu,Zhaofeng Wu,Roger P. Levy,Yoon Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究预训练语言模型是否在隐藏表征中学到了独立于字符串概率的“语法性”概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然语言模型能生成流畅文本并在受控最小对中区分合语法与不合语法句子，但其整体字符串概率并不能清晰地区分语法性与非语法性；因此作者希望检验模型内部是否隐含了不同于概率评分的语法性表征。

Method: 作者从自然文本语料出发，通过扰动构造合语法/合成非合语法句子数据集，并在语言模型隐藏层表示上训练线性探针；随后在人工构建的语法判断基准、语义合理性基准以及多语言语法性基准上评估探针，并与基于语言模型字符串概率的判断方法比较。

Result: 线性语法性探针能泛化到人工语法判断基准，并优于基于字符串概率的语法判断；在语义合理性最小对任务中，探针弱于字符串概率；英文训练的探针还表现出一定跨语言泛化能力，在多种语言语法性基准上优于字符串概率；探针分数与字符串概率仅弱相关。

Conclusion: 结果表明，预训练语言模型在隐藏层中一定程度上习得了隐式的语法性区分，这一区分不同于单纯的字符串概率或语义 plausibility。

Abstract: Grammaticality and likelihood are distinct notions in human language. Pretrained language models (LMs), which are probabilistic models of language fitted to maximize corpus likelihood, generate grammatically well-formed text and discriminate well between grammatical and ungrammatical sentences in tightly controlled minimal pairs. However, their string probabilities do not sharply discriminate between grammatical and ungrammatical sentences overall. But do LMs implicitly acquire a grammaticality distinction distinct from string probability? We explore this question through studying internal representations of LMs, by training a linear probe on a dataset of grammatical and (synthetic) ungrammatical sentences obtained by applying perturbations to a naturalistic text corpus. We find that this simple grammaticality probe generalizes to human-curated grammaticality judgment benchmarks and outperforms LM probability-based grammaticality judgments. When applied to semantic plausibility benchmarks, in which both members of a minimal pair are grammatical and differ in only plausibility, the probe however performs worse than string probability. The English-trained probe also exhibits nontrivial cross-lingual generalization, outperforming string probabilities on grammaticality benchmarks in numerous other languages. Additionally, probe scores correlate only weakly with string probabilities. These results collectively suggest that LMs acquire to some extent an implicit grammaticality distinction within their hidden layers.

</details>

### [124] [LCM: Lossless Context Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04050)
*Clint Ehrlich,Theodore Blackman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Lossless Context Management（LCM），一种用于大语言模型记忆管理的确定性架构；在长上下文编程任务评测中，LCM 增强的智能体 Volt 表现优于 Claude Code。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM 与编码智能体在超长上下文任务中面临上下文压缩、历史状态遗忘、检索不完整以及模型自主递归控制不稳定等问题。作者希望构建一种既能处理长上下文、又能保证历史信息可追溯和任务执行可终止的记忆架构。

Method: LCM 将递归式上下文操作拆解为两个由引擎管理的确定性机制：其一是递归上下文压缩，通过层级摘要 DAG 自动压缩旧消息，同时保留指向原始内容的无损指针；其二是递归任务划分，用引擎管理的并行原语（如 LLM-Map）替代模型自行编写循环。

Result: 在使用 Opus 4.6 的 OOLONG 长上下文评测中，LCM 增强的编码智能体 Volt 在 32K 到 1M token 的所有上下文长度上均超过 Claude Code。

Conclusion: LCM 证明并扩展了递归语言模型范式：通过将递归控制从模型生成转移到确定性引擎机制中，可以在牺牲部分灵活性的同时获得终止保证、短任务零额外连续性成本以及对全部历史状态的无损检索能力。

Abstract: We introduce Lossless Context Management (LCM), a deterministic architecture for LLM memory that outperforms Claude Code on long-context tasks. When benchmarked using Opus 4.6, our LCM-augmented coding agent, Volt, achieves higher scores than Claude Code on the OOLONG long-context eval, including at every context length between 32K and 1M tokens.
  LCM may be considered both a vindication and extension of the recursive paradigm pioneered by Recursive Language Models (RLMs). Our results demonstrate that recursive context manipulation can outperform not just conventional LLMs, but frontier coding agents with native file-system access.
  LCM departs from RLM by decomposing symbolic recursion into two deterministic, engine-managed mechanisms: recursive context compression, in which a hierarchical summary DAG automatically compacts older messages while retaining lossless pointers to every original; and recursive task partitioning, in which engine-managed parallel primitives like LLM-Map replace model-written loops. This trade-off, analogous to the move from GOTO to structured control flow in program-ming language design, sacrifices maximal flexibility for termination guarantees, zero-cost continuity on short tasks, and lossless retrievability of all prior state.

</details>


### [125] [Regularized Centered Emphatic Temporal Difference Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04100)
*Xingguo Chen,Chaohui Wu,Jinguo Ye,Chao Li,Shangdong Yang,Guang Yang,Tianyu Liang,Wenhao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出正则化强调时序差分学习（RETD），用于缓解离策略 TD 中强调权重带来的方差与稳定性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离策略 TD 学习结合函数逼近时存在稳定性、投影几何和方差控制之间的结构性权衡。ETD 通过 follow-on emphasis 改善离策略投影几何，但 follow-on trace 可能产生较高方差；而朴素的 Bellman 误差中心化扩展又可能破坏关键矩阵的正定性。

Method: 作者重新审视 Bellman-error centering，并指出朴素中心化 emphatic 方法会引入辅助耦合，导致 ETD 关键矩阵不再保持正定。为此提出 RETD：保留原有 follow-on trace，仅对辅助中心化递归进行正则化，相当于将耦合关键矩阵的右下块从 1 提升到 1+c；同时推导 RETD 核心矩阵并给出保守的充分收敛条件。

Result: 在线性离策略预测诊断任务上的实验表明，RETD 避免了朴素中心化 emphatic 学习的不稳定性，保持了较好的 emphatic 投影几何，并且在多个诊断任务中对正则化参数 c 呈现稳健的中间有效区间。

Conclusion: RETD 在不牺牲 ETD 几何优势的前提下，通过正则化中心化辅助递归改善稳定性和方差控制，为离策略 TD 学习中的中心化与强调机制结合提供了更可靠的方案。

Abstract: Off-policy temporal-difference (TD) learning with function approximation faces a structural tradeoff among stability, projection geometry, and variance control. Emphatic TD (ETD) improves the off-policy projection geometry through follow-on emphasis, but the follow-on trace can have high variance. We revisit this tradeoff through Bellman-error centering. Although centering naturally removes a common drift term from TD errors, we show that a naive centered emphatic extension introduces an auxiliary coupling that can destroy the positive-definiteness of the ETD key matrix. We propose \emph{Regularized Emphatic Temporal-Difference Learning} (RETD), which preserves the follow-on trace and regularizes only the auxiliary centering recursion, corresponding to lifting the lower-right block of the coupled key matrix from \(1\) to \(1+c\). We derive the RETD core matrix, prove convergence under a conservative sufficient regularization condition, and evaluate the method on diagnostic linear off-policy prediction tasks. The experiments show that RETD avoids the instability of naive centered emphatic learning, preserves favorable emphatic geometry, and exhibits a robust intermediate regime for the regularization parameter \(c\) across the diagnostics.

</details>


### [126] [ANDRE: An Attention-based Neuro-symbolic Differentiable Rule Extractor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04193)
*Iman Sharifi,Peng Wei,Saber Fallah*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 ANDRE：一种基于注意力的神经符号可微规则抽取框架，用连续规则空间与注意力逻辑算子学习可解释的一阶逻辑规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 ILP 方法在噪声与概率性数据场景下扩展性和鲁棒性不足：经典符号 ILP 依赖离散组合搜索，面对不确定性较脆弱；可微 ILP 常依赖预定义规则模板或不精确的模糊逻辑算子，可能出现梯度消失或逻辑语义近似不佳。

Method: ANDRE 通过注意力驱动的合取与析取算子替代固定规则模板和传统逻辑算子，在连续规则空间中优化一阶逻辑程序；模型可对谓词进行软选择、取反或排除，并近似逻辑 min-max 语义，以支持概率谓词赋值上的稳定、可解释推理。

Result: 在经典 ILP 基准、大规模知识库以及含概率谓词和噪声监督的合成数据集上，ANDRE 获得了有竞争力或更优的预测性能，并能在不确定条件下更可靠地恢复正确符号规则；在中等标签噪声下，相比现有可微 ILP 方法显著提升规则抽取质量与稳定性。

Conclusion: ANDRE 表明，基于注意力的可微逻辑算子可以在保持符号结构和可解释性的同时，提高 ILP 在概率、噪声和大规模场景中的学习能力与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Inductive Logic Programming (ILP) aims to learn interpretable first-order rules from data, but existing symbolic and neuro-symbolic approaches struggle to scale to noisy and probabilistic settings. Classical ILP relies on discrete combinatorial rule search and is brittle under uncertainty, while differentiable ILP methods typically depend on predefined rule templates or inaccurate fuzzy operators that suffer from vanishing gradients or poor approximation of logical structure when reasoning over probabilistic predicate valuations. This paper proposes an Attention-based Neuro-symbolic Differentiable Rule Extractor (ANDRE), a novel ILP framework that learns first-order logic programs by optimizing over a continuous rule space with attention-based logical operators. ANDRE replaces both rule templates and logical operators with fully differentiable, attention-driven conjunction and disjunction operators that approximate logical min-max semantics, enabling accurate, stable, and interpretable reasoning over probabilistic data. By softly selecting, negating, or excluding predicates within each rule, ANDRE supports flexible rule induction while preserving symbolic structure. Extensive experiments on classical ILP benchmarks, large-scale knowledge bases, and synthetic datasets with probabilistic predicates and noisy supervision demonstrate that ANDRE achieves competitive or superior predictive performance while reliably recovering correct symbolic rules under uncertainty. In particular, ANDRE remains robust to moderate label noise, substantially outperforming existing differentiable ILP methods in both rule extraction quality and stability.

</details>

*Lilin Xu,Bufang Yang,Siyang Jiang,Kaiwei Liu,Kaiyuan Hou,Yuang Fan,Hongkai Chen,Zhenyu Yan,Xiaofan Jiang*

Result: 在公开数据整理的数据集和真实 AR 眼镜测试平台采集的数据集上，Pro²Assist 相比最佳基线在程序动作理解准确率上提升超过 21%，主动辅助时机准确率最高达到基线的 2.29 倍；20 人用户研究中，90% 参与者认为该系统有用。

Abstract: Procedural tasks with multiple ordered steps are ubiquitous in daily life. However, existing systems primarily provide reactive guidance triggered by user queries, or limited proactive assistance for isolated short-term events rather than long-horizon procedural tasks. In this work, we introduce Pro$^2$Assist, a step-aware proactive assistant that continuously tracks fine-grained task progress and reasons over the user's evolving state to provide timely assistance throughout tasks. Pro$^2$Assist leverages multimodal data from augmented reality (AR) glasses to achieve motion-based perception. It then extracts step-oriented procedural context from multi-scale temporal dynamics and task-specific expert knowledge. Based on both sensory input and procedural context, Pro$^2$Assist performs continuous reasoning to infer user needs and display timely assistance on AR glasses. We evaluate Pro$^2$Assist using a dataset curated from public sources and a real-world dataset collected on our testbed with AR glasses. Extensive evaluations show that Pro$^2$Assist outperforms the best-performing baselines by over 21% in procedural action understanding accuracy, and it achieves up to 2.29x the proactive timing accuracy of baselines. A user study with 20 participants further shows that 90% find Pro$^2$Assist useful, indicating its effectiveness for real-world procedural assistance.

### [128] [Temporal Reasoning Is Not the Bottleneck: A Probabilistic Inconsistency Framework for Neuro-Symbolic QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04243)
*Tran Quang Liem*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文认为LLM在复杂时间推理中的主要瓶颈并非逻辑推理能力不足，而是非结构化文本到事件表示的转换不可靠；提出一种带概率不一致信号的神经符号QA框架来分离表示错误与推理错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有观点通常将LLM时间推理失败归因于自回归模型的逻辑演绎缺陷。作者希望重新检验这一假设，明确失败究竟来自推理模块本身，还是来自将自然语言文本解析为可推理结构时产生的表示偏差。

Method: 提出神经符号问答框架：先将非结构化文本提升为显式事件图与区间约束，再交由符号推理引擎处理；同时设计Probabilistic Inconsistency Signal（PIS），融合符号置信区间与基于LLM隐藏状态的证据深度学习不确定性，用于检测结构性错误并定位感知/抽取错误与推理错误。

Result: 在给定正确结构化表示时，系统在时间算术基准上达到1.0准确率（4000/4000），且假阳性和假阴性均为0；在更广泛的噪声注入QA场景中达到75.1%准确率，并能提供确定性的逐步失败定位。

Conclusion: 研究将时间QA的核心问题从“算法推理能力不足”重新定义为“结构对齐与表示可靠性问题”，表明可靠的神经符号AI需要重点提升文本到事件结构的抽取质量，并通过可验证推理链路实现错误隔离与诊断。

Abstract: Despite significant advances, large language models (LLMs) continue to exhibit brittle performance on complex temporal reasoning tasks. This failure mode is widely attributed to inherent deficits in autoregressive logical deduction. In this paper, we challenge this prevailing narrative, demonstrating that temporal reasoning is not the fundamental bottleneck; rather, the locus of failure lies in unstructured text-to-event representation. We introduce a novel neuro-symbolic question-answering framework governed by a Probabilistic Inconsistency Signal (PIS) that explicitly isolates perceptual errors from reasoning failures. By lifting unstructured text into explicit event graphs and interval constraints, our architecture strictly decouples semantic extraction from a symbolic reasoning engine. To robustly detect structural breaks, the PIS elegantly unifies symbolic credal intervals with epistemic neural uncertainty extracted via Evidential Deep Learning on LLM hidden states. Empirical evaluations reveal a striking paradigm shift: when provided with correct structural representations, our system's explicit proof traces achieve perfect 1.0 accuracy (4000/4000) and strictly zero false positives/negatives on temporal arithmetic benchmarks. On broader, noise-injected QA settings, the framework maintains a competitive 75.1\% accuracy while enabling deterministic, step-level failure localization. Ultimately, by isolating the representation bottleneck from the reasoning substrate, this work reframes temporal QA from an algorithmic reasoning challenge to a structural alignment problem, charting a verifiable path forward for reliable neuro-symbolic AI.

### [129] [Parallel Prefix Verification for Speculative Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04263)
*Yuncheng Yao,Yuxuan Xia,Shengjie Wang,Danyang Zhuo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PARSE 是一种通过并行前缀验证提升大语言模型推理速度的投机生成框架，可在语义/片段级别一次性识别最长有效前缀，并显著提高吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有投机解码主要受限于 token 级等价验证：目标模型需要逐 token 验证，导致接受长度较短、加速有限。语义或片段级验证虽可扩大接受粒度，但既有方法通常需要顺序验证多个片段，带来额外开销，削弱实际收益。因此，论文希望在语义级验证中消除顺序检查瓶颈。

Method: PARSE 首先由草稿模型生成完整草稿，然后让目标模型通过自定义 attention mask 在单次前向传播中并行评估多个前缀的正确性，直接定位最大有效前缀。该方法避免逐段顺序验证，并且可与 token 级投机解码方法（如 EAGLE-3）组合使用。

Result: 实验显示，PARSE 相比目标模型实现 1.25× 到 4.3× 的吞吐量提升；与 EAGLE-3 组合后达到 1.6× 到 4.5× 的吞吐量提升，同时精度退化可以忽略。

Conclusion: 并行前缀验证能够有效降低语义级投机验证开销，提高接受粒度与推理吞吐，是一种通用且可组合的 LLM 推理加速方法。

Abstract: We introduce PARSE (PArallel pRefix Speculative Engine), a speculative generation framework that accelerates large language model (LLM) inference by parallelizing prefix verification on a semantic level. Existing speculative decoding methods are fundamentally limited by token-level equivalence: the target model must verify each token, leading to short acceptance lengths and modest speedups. Moving to semantic or segment-level verification can substantially increase acceptance granularity, but prior approaches rely on sequential verification, introducing significant overhead and limiting practical gains. PARSE introduces parallel prefix verification, enabling semantic-level verification without sequential checks. Given a full draft from a draft model, the target model evaluates correctness across multiple prefixes in a single forward pass using a custom attention mask, directly identifying the maximal valid prefix. This eliminates sequential segment verification, and makes verification compute-efficient. PARSE is orthogonal to token-level speculative decoding and can be composed with it for additional gains. Across models and benchmarks, PARSE delivers $1.25\times$ to $4.3\times$ throughput gain over the target model, and $1.6\times$ to $4.5\times$ when composed with EAGLE-3, all with negligible accuracy degradation. This demonstrates parallel prefix verification as an effective, general approach to accelerating LLM inference.

### [130] [Agent Island: A Saturation- and Contamination-Resistant Benchmark from Multiagent Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04312)
*Connacher Murphy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Agent Island，一个多智能体仿真动态基准，用竞争式环境评估语言模型能力，并用贝叶斯 Plackett-Luce 模型进行技能排名。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态能力基准容易出现饱和和数据污染，难以长期、可靠地追踪语言模型能力进展，因此需要一种更动态、抗污染、可持续区分模型表现的评测方式。

Method: 构建多人仿真环境 Agent Island，让语言模型智能体在合作、竞争与说服场景中相互博弈；采用胜者通吃机制避免固定题集限制；用贝叶斯 Plackett-Luce 排名模型估计玩家技能并量化不确定性；同时发布游戏日志数据用于行为分析。

Result: 在 999 局游戏、49 个模型中，openai/gpt-5.5 以 posterior mean skill 5.64 显著领先；第二名 openai/gpt-5.2 为 3.10，第三名 openai/gpt-5.3-codex 为 2.86。行为分析发现模型在最终投票中对同一提供商 finalist 的支持概率高出 8.3 个百分点，且该偏好在不同提供商间不一致。

Conclusion: Agent Island 展示了动态、多智能体基准可缓解传统静态基准的饱和与污染问题，并能同时评估模型能力与交互行为偏差；但其排名结果依赖环境设计、博弈规则和参赛模型池，需进一步验证泛化性。

Abstract: Static capabilities benchmarks suffer from saturation and contamination, making it difficult to track capabilities progress over time. We introduce Agent Island, a multiplayer simulation environment in which language-model agents compete in a game of interagent cooperation, conflict, and persuasion. The environment yields a dynamic benchmark designed to mitigate both saturation and contamination; new models can always outperform the current leading player in this winner-take-all game, and agents compete against other adaptive agents rather than face a fixed task set. We rank players with a Bayesian Plackett-Luce model, allowing us to quantify uncertainty in player skill. In 999 games involving 49 unique models, openai/gpt-5.5 dominates its peers with a posterior mean skill of 5.64, compared with 3.10 for the second-ranked model, openai/gpt-5.2, and 2.86 for the third-ranked model, openai/gpt-5.3-codex. We release the game logs as a dataset for analyses of model behavior. As an example, we investigate same-provider preference in final-round votes and find that models are 8.3 p.p. more likely to support a same-provider finalist than finalists from other providers. This preference is not uniform across providers: among separately estimated providers, the effect is strongest for OpenAI models and weakest for Anthropic models.

*Enrico Vompa,Tanel Tammet*

Conclusion: 隐式 Transformer 推理具备一定算法化演绎能力和宽度/结构泛化潜力，但其深度泛化仍受限；显式 CoT 在提升深层推理外推方面仍是关键机制。

### [132] [When Context Hurts: The Crossover Effect of Knowledge Transfer on Multi-Agent Design Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04361)
*Saranyan Vigraham*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文发现多智能体软件设计中“更多上下文更好”的假设并不总成立；上下文是否有益取决于任务在无上下文条件下的基线探索程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体编排普遍假设向智能体注入更多上下文或知识工件会提升表现，但这一假设缺乏系统验证，尤其是在多智能体软件设计任务中的效果可能因任务而异。

Method: 作者在10个软件设计任务、7种上下文注入条件下进行了超过2700次运行，比较不同工件类型对设计探索的影响；同时用无上下文基线探索程度作为预测变量，并通过改变提示词中的收敛压力来探查作用机制。

Result: 实验发现明显的交叉效应：同一类上下文工件在某些任务上可将权衡覆盖提升最高20倍，但在另一些任务上会导致最高46%的下降；部分任务中，无关文档的效果等于或优于所有相关工件。无上下文基线探索程度能显著预测上下文效果方向，Pearson r=-0.82，p<0.001。

Conclusion: 上下文注入不应被视为通用策略，而应按任务条件化使用；一次低成本的无上下文试运行可以作为诊断手段，预测知识工件会帮助还是损害特定任务。

Abstract: The prevailing assumption in agent orchestration is that more context is better. We test this on multi-agent software design across 10 tasks, 7 context-injection conditions, and over 2,700 runs, and find a crossover effect: the same artifact type improves design exploration on some tasks (up to 20$\times$ tradeoff coverage) and actively degrades it on others (up to 46% reduction). On several tasks, an irrelevant document performs as well as or better than every relevant artifact. The direction is predicted by a single measurable variable--baseline exploration without context--with Pearson $r = -0.82$ ($p < 0.001$). Probing the mechanism by manipulating convergence pressure through prompt design reveals two distinct regimes: convergence driven by training data priors (natural) responds to artifact disruption, while convergence driven by explicit instructions (induced) does not. The implication is that context injection should be conditional, not universal: one no-context trial is a cheap diagnostic that predicts whether knowledge artifacts will help or hurt a given task.

</details>


### [133] [Deployment-Relevant Alignment Cannot Be Inferred from Model-Level Evaluation Alone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04454)
*Varad Vishwarupe,Nigel Shadbolt,Marina Jirotka,Ivan Flechais*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文主张机器学习对齐评估不应仅停留在模型级基准分数，而应按证据收集层级区分为模型级、响应级、交互级和部署级，并转向系统级评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有有影响力的对齐基准通常在固定输入下评估模型输出，如真实性、指令遵循或偏好比较，并据此支持部署对齐声明；作者认为这种模型级评估不足以推断真实部署中的对齐表现。

Method: 论文开展两项研究：其一，对11个对齐基准进行结构化审计，并扩展至16个基准语料，使用八维度量表双人编码，Cohen's kappa为0.87；其二，进行盲法跨模型压力测试，覆盖三个前沿模型、四种脚手架和180段交互记录。

Result: 审计发现所有考察基准均缺乏面向用户的验证支持，过程可控性也几乎缺失；少数交互式基准覆盖零散，且测量内容主要由基准构造方式而非数据来源决定。压力测试显示同一验证脚手架可使某一模型的验证支持达到上限，却对另一模型几乎无影响，说明脚手架效果依赖模型。

Conclusion: 论文建议采用系统级评估议程：用对齐画像替代单一分数，使用固定脚手架协议提升交互评估可比性，并通过报告模板明确评估证据与部署声明之间的推断距离。

Abstract: Alignment evaluation in machine learning has largely become evaluation of models. Influential benchmarks score model outputs under fixed inputs, such as truthfulness, instruction following, or pairwise preference, and these scores are often used to support claims about deployed alignment. This paper argues that deployment-relevant alignment cannot be inferred from model-level evaluation alone. Alignment claims should instead be indexed to the level at which evidence is collected: model-level, response-level, interaction-level, or deployment-level. Two studies support this position. First, a structured audit of eleven alignment benchmarks, extended to a sixteen-benchmark corpus, dual-coded against an eight-dimension rubric with Cohen's kappa = 0.87, finds that user-facing verification support is absent across every benchmark examined, while process steerability is nearly absent. The few interactional benchmarks identified, including tau-bench, CURATe, Rifts, and Common Ground, remain fragmented in coverage, and benchmark construction rather than data source determines what is measured. Second, a blinded cross-model stress test using 180 transcripts across three frontier models and four scaffolds finds that the same verification scaffold raises one model's verification support to ceiling while leaving another categorically unchanged. This shows that scaffold efficacy is model-dependent and that the gap identified by the audit cannot be closed at the model level alone. We propose a system-level evaluation agenda: alignment profiles instead of single scores, fixed-scaffolding protocols for comparable interactional evaluation, and reporting templates that make the inferential distance between evaluation evidence and deployment claims explicit.

</details>


### [134] [How Does Thinking Mode Change LLM Moral Judgments? A Controlled Instant-vs-Thinking Comparison Across Five Frontier Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04488)
*Sai Sourabh Madur*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究比较同一模型在即时模式与推理模式下的道德判断差异，发现总体二元判决一致性几乎不变，但在存在分歧的场景中，推理模式可缩小跨模型分歧，并减少部分模型的人口属性相关判断不一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大模型提供商开放“推理/思考模式”，需要评估这种模式是否会改变同一模型检查点的道德判断，尤其是是否影响模型间一致性、敏感属性相关一致性以及模型自称采用的伦理框架。

Method: 研究在100个道德判断场景上测试五个前沿推理训练大模型，对比即时模式与思考模式的二元 verdict、模型间一致性、争议场景表现、人口属性判断不一致性，以及自我标注伦理框架的变化；使用Krippendorff's alpha和平均成对一致性等指标。

Result: 总体二元判断一致性在两种模式下都较高且统计上不可区分，Krippendorff's alpha分别为0.78和0.79；分歧主要集中在21个模型争议场景，即时模式alpha仅0.08；在这些场景中，推理模式将平均成对一致性从10分中的5.4提高到6.7；推理还在五个模型中的三个中降低人口属性相关判断不一致性，且没有模型出现增加；伦理框架自我标签变化比二元 verdict 更频繁。

Conclusion: 启用推理模式并不会显著改变模型整体二元道德判决，但可在高争议场景中提升跨模型一致性，并可能改善部分公平性相关稳定性；同时，推理更容易改变模型对伦理理由或框架的表述，而非最终判决。

Abstract: We evaluate whether enabling provider-exposed reasoning mode changes moral judgments within the same model checkpoint. Across 100 moral-judgment scenarios and five frontier reasoning-trained LLMs (Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT 5.5, Gemini 3 Flash, DeepSeek V3.1, and Qwen3.5 397B), aggregate binary-verdict agreement remains high and statistically indistinguishable between instant and thinking modes (Krippendorff's alpha = 0.78 vs. 0.79). However, disagreement is concentrated in 21 model-disputed scenarios, where instant-mode agreement is near chance (alpha = 0.08). On these scenarios, reasoning directionally narrows cross-model disagreement, increasing mean pairwise agreement from 5.4 to 6.7 out of 10. Reasoning also reduces demographic-judgment inconsistency in three of five models and does not increase it for any model. Across all five model families, reasoning changes self-labeled ethical frameworks more often than binary verdicts.

</details>


### [135] [From Parameter Dynamics to Risk Scoring : Quantifying Sample-Level Safety Degradation in LLM Fine-tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04572)
*Xiao Wang,Yifei Zhang,YongKang Liu,Xiaocui Yang,Zihan Wang,Shi Feng,Daling Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究LLM安全对齐在良性微调中退化的动态机制，并提出SQSD对训练样本的安全退化风险进行量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多比较微调前后的参数或隐藏状态，忽略微调过程中的动态演化，因而难以解释少量良性样本为何会显著削弱模型安全行为。

Method: 作者从参数动态角度分析发现，良性微调会使参数逐步向“风险对齐方向”累积漂移；据此提出Sample-Level Quantification of Safety Degradation（SQSD），通过衡量单个样本诱导的参数更新在风险方向与安全方向上的投影差，为每个样本计算连续风险分数。

Result: 在多个模型和数据集上的实验表明，SQSD能够有效量化样本级微调风险，并在不同模型架构、参数规模和参数高效微调方法之间具有较强迁移性。

Conclusion: 安全退化可被理解为微调过程中参数向不安全方向的累积漂移；SQSD为识别高风险训练样本、提升微调安全性提供了可操作的样本级评估工具。

Abstract: Safety alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) is extremely fragile, as fine-tuning on a small number of benign samples can erase safety behaviors learned from millions of preference examples. Existing studies attempt to explain this phenomenon by comparing parameters and hidden states before and after fine-tuning, but overlook their dynamic evolution during fine-tuning. In this paper, we uncover a critical mechanism underlying safety degradation by analyzing parameter dynamics, where benign fine-tuning causes parameters to cumulatively drift toward danger-aligned directions, progressively undermining the model's safety. This finding suggests that samples contributing more to this drift has greater fine-tuning risks. Based on this insight, we propose a method of Sample-Level Quantification of Safety Degradation (SQSD), which quantifies the influence of each training sample on safety degradation. Specifically, SQSD computes continuous risk scores to samples by measuring their induced parameter updates' projection difference between danger and safety directions. Extensive experiments across multiple models and datasets demonstrate that SQSD effectively quantifies sample-level fine-tuning risks and exhibits strong transferability across model architectures, parameter scales, and parameter-efficient methods.

</details>

However, current deep learning-based HAR models often struggle with heavy reliance on labeled data, position-specific ambiguity, and a lack of transparent reasoning. Inspired by the advanced agents framework, which emulates a collaborative agent using Large Language Models (LLMs), we propose SensingAgents, a novel multi-agent system for robust IMU activity recognition. SensingAgents organizes LLM-powered agents into specialized roles: a group of Analyst Agents for position-specific sensor analysis (arm, wrist, belt, pocket), a pair of Advocate Agents that resolves sensor conflicts through dynamic and static dialectical debates, and a Decision Agent that ensures reliability under sensor drift or failure. Evaluation on the Shoaib dataset demonstrates that SensingAgents significantly outperforms state-of-the-art single-agent and multi-agent LLM models, achieving an accuracy of 79.5% in a zero setting--29% higher than existing agent models and 9.4% higher than deep learning baselines--particularly in complex scenarios where multi-sensor data is conflicting or noisy. *Miao Wang,Yuling Shi,Yijiang Li,Yeheng Chen,Xiaodong Gu,Bin Li,Bo Gao,Yaduan Ruan*

Main category: cs.AI

This structure promotes human-like sensory grounding by compelling the model to first attend to visual cues, then form internal interpretations, and finally generate context-appropriate dialogue.
  EBM-RL integrates four complementary rewards: (i) CLIP-based scene-text alignment to improve ambiance and emotion; (ii) a Perceptual-Cognitive reward that encourages [perception] and [think] processes that increase the likelihood of the reference response; (iii) answer accuracy to ensure faithfulness; and (iv) a dense format reward to enforce the desired structured output.

Beyond the role-playing domain, EBM-RL also exhibits strong zero-shot generalization: without any additional fine-tuning, it consistently improves performance on out-of-domain VideoQA benchmarks. ### [138] [AgentTrust: Runtime Safety Evaluation and Interception for AI Agent Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04785)
*Chenglin Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 AgentTrust：一种在 AI Agent 工具调用执行前进行拦截与风险判定的运行时安全层，可输出 allow、warn、block、review 等结构化决策，并在两个基准上取得较高准确率与低延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代 AI Agent 会通过文件操作、命令行、HTTP 请求、数据库查询等工具调用产生真实世界副作用；单次不安全操作可能导致删除、凭据泄露或数据外泄等不可逆损害。现有方案存在不足：事后评测无法阻止执行、静态规则难以处理混淆和多步上下文、沙箱只能限制执行环境而不能理解动作语义。

Method: AgentTrust 在工具调用执行前进行运行时拦截，结合 shell 去混淆归一化器、SafeFix 安全替代建议、RiskChain 多步攻击链检测，以及带缓存机制的 LLM-as-Judge 来处理模糊输入，最终返回 allow/warn/block/review 的结构化 verdict。

Conclusion: AgentTrust 展示了运行时、语义感知的工具调用安全防护在 AI Agent 部署中的实用价值，能够在执行前识别高风险动作并提供替代建议；其开源发布和 MCP server 支持有助于与现有 Agent 生态集成。

Abstract: Modern AI agents execute real-world side effects through tool calls such as file operations, shell commands, HTTP requests, and database queries. A single unsafe action, including accidental deletion, credential exposure, or data exfiltration, can cause irreversible harm. Existing defenses are incomplete: post-hoc benchmarks measure behavior after execution, static guardrails miss obfuscation and multi-step context, and infrastructure sandboxes constrain where code runs without understanding what an action means.
  We present AgentTrust, a runtime safety layer that intercepts agent tool calls before execution and returns a structured verdict: allow, warn, block, or review. AgentTrust combines a shell deobfuscation normalizer, SafeFix suggestions for safer alternatives, RiskChain detection for multi-step attack chains, and a cache-aware LLM-as-Judge for ambiguous inputs.
  We release a 300-scenario benchmark across six risk categories and an additional 630 independently constructed real-world adversarial scenarios. On the internal benchmark, the production-only ruleset achieves 95.0% verdict accuracy and 73.7% risk-level accuracy at low-millisecond end-to-end latency. On the 630-scenario benchmark, evaluated under a patched ruleset and not claimed as zero-shot, AgentTrust achieves 96.7% verdict accuracy, including about 93% on shell-obfuscated payloads. AgentTrust is released under the AGPL-3.0 license and provides a Model Context Protocol server for MCP-compatible agents.

Evaluating agent security is inherently challenging, as agents operate in dynamic, untrusted environments involving external tools, heterogeneous data sources, and frequent user interactions. However, realistic, controllable, and reproducible environments for large-scale risk assessment remain largely underexplored. Using DTap-Red, we curate DTap-Bench, a large-scale red-teaming dataset comprising high-quality instances across domains, each paired with a verifiable judge to automatically validate attack outcomes. ### [140] [Strat-Reasoner: Reinforcing Strategic Reasoning of LLMs in Multi-Agent Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04906)
*Yidong He,Yutao Lai,Pengxu Yang,Jiarui Gan,Jiexin Wang,Yi Cai,Mengchen Zhao*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM 在部分推理任务上表现良好，但在多智能体博弈中，由于其他智能体策略的非平稳性，模型难以评估自身多步推理过程并进行准确的信用分配。传统单智能体 RL 及其多智能体扩展通常未将其他智能体的推理过程显式纳入自身推理，因此难以应对联合策略决定最终结果的场景。

Method: 论文提出 Strat-Reasoner：首先设计递归推理范式，使一个智能体在推理时整合其他智能体的推理过程；其次使用集中式 Chain-of-Thought 比较模块，为中间推理序列提供更有效的奖励信号；最后计算混合优势估计，并采用组相对强化学习方法优化 LLM 策略。

Conclusion: 该工作说明，在多智能体环境中显式建模其他智能体的推理过程，并结合集中式推理质量评估与改进的 RL 优化机制，可以有效增强 LLM 的战略推理能力。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) excel in certain reasoning tasks, they struggle in multi-agent games where the final outcome depends on the joint strategies of all agents. In multi-agent games, the non-stationarity of other agents brings significant challenges on the evaluation of the reasoning process and the credit assignment over multiple reasoning steps. Existing single-agent reinforcement learning (RL) approaches and their multi-agent extensions fail to address these challenges as they do not incorporate other agents in the reasoning process. In this work, we propose Strat-Reasoner, a novel RL-based framework that improves LLMs' strategic reasoning ability in multi-agent games. We introduce a novel recursive reasoning paradigm where an agent's reasoning also integrates other agents' reasoning processes. To provide effective reward signals for the intermediate reasoning sequences, we employ a centralized Chain-of-Thought (CoT) comparison module to evaluate the reasoning quality. Finally, we compute an accurate hybrid advantage and develop a group-relative RL approach to optimize the LLM policy. Experimental results show that Strat-Reasoner substantially improves strategic abilities of underlying LLMs, achieving 22.1\% average performance improvements across various multi-agent games.
