### [141] [A Foundation Model for Zero-Shot Logical Rule Induction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04916)
*Yin Jun Phua*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 Neural Rule Inducer（NRI），一种用于零样本规则归纳的预训练模型，通过领域无关的统计特征表示文字，并以可微规则执行实现端到端训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有归纳逻辑编程方法多为传导式，学习到的参数绑定于特定谓词，面对新任务通常需要重新训练，限制了跨任务泛化与零样本规则归纳能力。

Method: NRI 不直接编码文字身份，而使用类别条件率、熵、共现等领域无关统计属性表示文字；模型包含统计编码器和并行槽位式解码器，以保持逻辑析取的置换不变性；采用 Product T-norm 松弛实现可微规则执行，并仅基于预测准确率进行端到端训练。

Result: 作者在规则恢复、标签噪声鲁棒性、虚假相关鲁棒性以及真实世界基准的零样本迁移上评估 NRI，摘要声称模型表现出跨任务泛化潜力。

Abstract: Inductive Logic Programming (ILP) learns interpretable logical rules from data. Existing methods are transductive: their learned parameters are bound to specific predicates and require retraining for each new task. We introduce Neural Rule Inducer (NRI), a pretrained model for zero-shot rule induction. Rather than encoding literal identities, NRI represents literals using domain-agnostic statistical properties such as class-conditional rates, entropy, and co-occurrence, which generalize across variable identities and counts without retraining. The model consists of a statistical encoder and a parallel slot-based decoder. Parallel decoding preserves the permutation invariance of logical disjunction; an autoregressive decoder would instead impose an arbitrary clause order. Product T-norm relaxation makes rule execution differentiable, allowing end-to-end training on prediction accuracy alone. We evaluate NRI on rule recovery, robustness to label noise and spurious correlations, and zero-shot transfer to real-world benchmarks, and we believe this work opens up the possibility of foundation models for symbolic reasoning. Code and the reference checkpoint are available at https://github.com/phuayj/neural-rule-inducer.

### [142] [On-line Learning in Tree MDPs by Treating Policies as Bandit Arms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04979)
*Anvay Shah,Ramsundar Anandanarayanan,Sharayu Moharir,Shivaram Kalyanakrishnan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究树结构有限时域MDP（T-MDP）的在线学习问题，提出可将LUCB/UCB等多臂老虎机算法以“策略为臂”应用于T-MDP，并通过共享数据构造置信界，使其在指数级策略空间下仍可多项式实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: T-MDP可自然刻画具有完美回忆、面对静态对手的序贯博弈抽象，但其策略数量随状态数指数增长，直接把每个策略视为一个臂会导致存储和计算不可行。因此需要设计既利用经典bandit方法、又能避免指数复杂度的在线学习算法。

Method: 作者将每个完整策略视为一个bandit臂，分别在PAC与遗憾最小化框架下使用LUCB和UCB思想。核心方法是利用不同策略在树上共享的状态-动作轨迹数据，构造可复用的置信上/下界，并通过动态规划或树结构计算实现策略选择，从而保持多项式内存与单步计算复杂度。

Result: 理论上，论文给出了实例依赖的样本复杂度与遗憾上界，其复杂度项按终止状态的gap求和，而不是按指数数量的策略求和。实验上，在一组隐藏信息博弈任务中，所提算法稳定优于已有替代方法。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，尽管T-MDP的策略空间指数巨大，经典bandit算法仍可通过结构化置信界和数据共享被高效扩展到树结构MDP；其理论界限更精细，实践表现也更优。

Abstract: A Tree Markov Decision Problem (T-MDP) is a finite-horizon MDP with a starting state $s_{1}$, in which every state is reachable from $s_{1}$ through exactly one state-action trajectory. T-MDPs arise naturally as abstractions of decision making in sequential games with perfect recall, against stationary opponents. We consider the problem of on-line learning in T-MDPs, both in the PAC and the regret-minimisation regimes. We show that well-known bandit algorithms -- \textsc{Lucb} and \textsc{Ucb} -- can be applied on T-MDPs by treating each policy as an arm. The apparent technical challenge in this approach is that the number of policies is exponential in the number of states. Our main innovation is in the design of confidence bounds based on data shared by the policies, so that the bandit algorithms can yet be implemented with polynomial memory and per-step computation. We obtain instance-dependent upper bounds on sample complexity and regret that sum a ``gap term'' from every terminal state, rather than every policy. Empirically, our algorithms consistently outperform available alternatives on a suite of hidden-information games.

</details>


### [143] [Uno-Orchestra: Parsimonious Agent Routing via Selective Delegation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05007)
*Zhiqing Cui,Haotong Xie,Jiahao Yuan,Cheng Yang,Hanqing Wang,Yuxin Wu,Yifan Wu,Siru Zhong,Tao Yu,Yifu Guo,Siyu Zhang,Xinlei Yu,Qibing Ren,Usman Naseem*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Uno-Orchestra 提出统一的 LLM 多智能体编排策略，在同一目标下联合学习任务是否/如何分解、子任务分派给何种模型与推理原语，并在多类基准上实现更高准确率与更低成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 LLM 多智能体系统通常依赖刚性的编排方式：要么进行扁平的逐查询路由，要么采用人工设计的任务分解流程。这使得分解深度、工作器选择与推理预算无法在统一目标下联合优化，限制了准确率与成本效率。

Method: 论文提出 Uno-Orchestra：一个统一编排策略，可选择性地将任务分解，并把每个子任务分派给可用的（模型，推理原语）组合。该策略通过基于真实 worker 交互的精选强化学习轨迹进行联合学习，从而同时优化分解决策与调度决策。

Result: 在覆盖数学、代码、知识、长上下文和智能体工具使用的 13 个基准套件上，与 22 个基线比较，Uno-Orchestra 达到 77.0% macro pass@1，约比最强 workflow 基线高 16%，同时单查询成本约低一个数量级。

Conclusion: Uno-Orchestra 推进了选择性委派场景下的准确率—效率前沿，表明统一学习式编排比固定路由或手工分解更能兼顾性能与成本。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) multi-agent systems typically rely on rigid orchestration, committing either to flat per-query routing or to hand-engineered task decomposition, so decomposition depth, worker choice, and inference budget are not jointly optimized under one objective. We introduce Uno-Orchestra, a unified orchestration policy that selectively decomposes a task and dispatches each subtask to an admissible (model, primitive) pair, with both decisions learned together from curated RL trajectories grounded in real worker interactions. Against 22 baselines on a 13-benchmark suite spanning math, code, knowledge, long-context, and agentic tool-use, Uno-Orchestra reaches 77.0% macro pass@1, roughly 16% above the strongest workflow baseline, at roughly an order of magnitude lower per-query cost, advancing the accuracy-efficiency frontier of selective delegation.

</details>


### [144] [Position: Embodied AI Requires a Privacy-Utility Trade-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05017)
*Xiaoliang Fan,Jiarui Chen,Zhuodong Liu,Ziqi Yang,Peixuan Xu,Ruimin Shen,Junhui Liu,Jianzhong Qi,Cheng Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出SPINE框架，主张具身AI隐私应作为贯穿全生命周期的架构级约束，而非各阶段的局部补丁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具身AI正从仿真走向真实家庭等敏感环境，但现有研究多在指令、感知、规划、交互等孤立阶段优化能力，忽视高频部署中跨阶段耦合导致的不可逆隐私泄露风险。

Method: 作者提出Secure Privacy Integration in Next-generation Embodied AI（SPINE）统一框架，将隐私建模为动态控制信号，分解EAI流水线各阶段，并通过多准则隐私分类矩阵协调不同阶段边界上的上下文敏感性与隐私约束传播。

Result: 通过初步仿真与真实案例研究，论文概念性展示隐私约束如何向下游传播并改变系统行为，说明仅依赖碎片化隐私补丁不足以应对系统性隐私风险。

Conclusion: 论文认为未来具身AI需要将隐私纳入生命周期级架构设计，在保证功能性的同时实现跨阶段、上下文感知的安全隐私治理。

Abstract: Embodied AI (EAI) systems are rapidly transitioning from simulations into real-world domestic and other sensitive environments. However, recent EAI solutions have largely demonstrated advancements within isolated stages such as instruction, perception, planning and interaction, without considering their coupled privacy implications in high-frequency deployments where privacy leakage is often irreversible. This position paper argues that optimizing these components independently creates a systemic privacy crisis when deployed in sensitive settings, thereby advancing the position that privacy in EAI is a life cycle-level architectural constraint rather than a stage-local feature. To address these challenges, we propose Secure Privacy Integration in Next-generation Embodied AI (SPINE), a unified privacy-aware framework that treats privacy as a dynamic control signal governing cross-stage coupling throughout the entire EAI life cycle. SPINE decomposes the EAI pipeline into various stages and establishes a multi-criterion privacy classification matrix to orchestrate contextual sensitivity across stage boundaries. We conduct preliminary simulation and real-world case studies to conceptually validate how privacy constraints propagate downstream to reshape system behavior, illustrating the insufficiency of fragmented privacy patches and motivating future research directions into secure yet functional embodied AI systems. We detail the SPINE framework and case studies at https://github.com/rminshen03/EAI_Privacy_Position.

</details>


### [145] [Executable World Models for ARC-AGI-3 in the Era of Coding Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05138)
*Sergey Rodionov*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文评估了一个面向 ARC-AGI-3 的初始编码智能体系统：通过可执行 Python 世界模型、基于历史观察的验证、面向简洁抽象的重构以及模型内规划来行动；在 25 个公开游戏上取得一定基线效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ARC-AGI-3 需要具备跨游戏泛化能力的智能体。作者希望验证一种不依赖手写游戏特定逻辑、以可执行世界模型和验证机制为核心的方法，是否能作为通用基线并展现解决任务的潜力。

Method: 系统采用脚本化控制器、预定义世界模型接口、验证程序和计划执行器。智能体维护可执行 Python 世界模型，用既往观察进行一致性验证，并通过重构趋向更简单的抽象，作为近似 MDL 式简洁性偏置；随后在该模型中规划再执行动作。每次 playthrough 使用全新的智能体实例，避免访问先前运行的文件或对话状态。

Result: 在 25 个公开 ARC-AGI-3 游戏中，系统完全解决 7 个游戏；在 6 个游戏上 Relative Human Action Efficiency（RHAE）超过 75%；平均逐游戏 RHAE 为 32.58%。部分游戏进行了多次独立运行以展示运行间差异。

Conclusion: 结果表明，在无游戏特定代码条件下，验证器驱动的可执行世界模型可作为 ARC-AGI-3 的通用基线，并初步显示出潜力；但私有验证集表现尚未测试，结论仍属初步。

Abstract: We evaluate an initial coding-agent system for ARC-AGI-3 in which the agent maintains an executable Python world model, verifies it against previous observations, refactors it toward simpler abstractions as a practical proxy for an MDL-like simplicity bias, and plans through the model before acting. The system is intentionally direct: it uses a scripted controller, predefined world-model interfaces, verifier programs, and a plan executor, but no hand-coded game-specific logic. We report results on the 25 public ARC-AGI-3 games. Each recorded playthrough uses a fresh agent instance with no access to previous playthrough-specific files or conversation state. Most games have a single recorded playthrough; for a few games, we report multiple independent fresh-agent playthroughs to expose run-to-run variability. The agent fully solved 7 games, achieved a Relative Human Action Efficiency greater than 75%, on 6 games, and obtained a mean per-game RHAE of 32.58%. Because the system uses no game-specific code, it can serve as a game-general baseline for ARC-AGI-3. Performance on the private validation set remains to be tested. Overall, the results provide preliminary evidence that verifier-driven executable world models are a promising approach for ARC-AGI-3 agents.

</details>


### [146] [LongSeeker: Elastic Context Orchestration for Long-Horizon Search Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05191)
*Yijun Lu,Rui Ye,Yuwen Du,Jiajun Wang,Songhua Liu,Siheng Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出 Context-ReAct，一种用于长程搜索智能体的自适应上下文编排范式，并基于其训练 LongSeeker，在多个搜索基准上显著优于对比系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长程搜索智能体在推理、调用工具和观察信息时会快速积累工作上下文；简单保留所有中间内容会导致上下文膨胀、成本上升，并增加错误与幻觉风险。因此需要一种能根据任务相关性动态调整信息粒度的上下文管理机制。

Method: 作者提出 Context-ReAct，将推理、上下文管理与工具使用整合到统一循环中，并设计五种原子操作：Skip、Compress、Rollback、Snippet、Delete，用于跳过、压缩、回滚、提取片段和删除上下文内容。同时证明 Compress 操作具有表达完备性，其他操作提供效率与保真度保障。基于该范式，作者用 1 万条合成轨迹对 Qwen3-30B-A3B 进行微调，得到 LongSeeker。

Result: LongSeeker 在四个代表性搜索基准上取得较好表现，其中 BrowseComp 为 61.5%，BrowseComp-ZH 为 62.5%，明显超过 Tongyi DeepResearch 的 43.2%/46.7% 和 AgentFold 的 36.2%/47.3%。

Conclusion: 实验表明，自适应上下文管理能够提升长程搜索智能体的可靠性与效率。通过主动塑造工作记忆，智能体可以更好地保留关键证据、压缩已解决信息、丢弃无效分支，并降低生成成本和幻觉风险。

Abstract: Long-horizon search agents must manage a rapidly growing working context as they reason, call tools, and observe information. Naively accumulating all intermediate content can overwhelm the agent, increasing costs and the risk of errors. We propose that effective context management should be adaptive: parts of the agent's trajectory are maintained at different levels of detail depending on their current relevance to the task. To operationalize this principle, we introduce Context-ReAct, a general agentic paradigm for elastic context orchestration that integrates reasoning, context management, and tool use in a unified loop. Context-ReAct provides five atomic operations: Skip, Compress, Rollback, Snippet and Delete, which allow the agent to dynamically reshape its working context, preserving important evidence, summarizing resolved information, discarding unhelpful branches, and controlling context size. We prove that the Compress operator is expressively complete, while the other specialized operators provide efficiency and fidelity guarantees that reduce generation cost and hallucination risk. Building on this paradigm, we develop LongSeeker, a long-horizon search agent fine-tuned from Qwen3-30B-A3B on 10k synthesized trajectories. Across four representative search benchmarks, LongSeeker achieves 61.5% on BrowseComp and 62.5% on BrowseComp-ZH, substantially outperforming Tongyi DeepResearch (43.2% and 46.7%) and AgentFold (36.2% and 47.3%). These results highlight the potential of adaptive context management, showing that agents can achieve more reliable and efficient long-horizon reasoning by actively shaping their working memory.

</details>

### [147] [Z-Opt: A Near-Optimal Reduced-Complexity Two-Dimensional Grassmannian Constellation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04545)
*Kotaro Shigenaga,Hiroki Iimori,Yuto Hama,Chandan Pradhan,Szabolcs Malomsoky,Naoki Ishikawa*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出两种用于二维空间中一维子空间 Grassmannian 星座的构造方法 S-Opt 与 Z-Opt，并设计低复杂度检测器；通过 Bloch 球上的几何等价关系实现接近或达到理论距离上界的星座设计，同时保持与 GLRT 相同的检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Grassmannian 星座在高信噪比非相干 Rayleigh 衰落通信中可达到容量，但高效构造和低复杂度检测仍具挑战。作者希望利用 Bloch 球几何表示简化 Grassmannian 星座的设计与检测。

Method: 将 \mathcal{G}(2,1) 上的弦距离映射为 Bloch 球上的欧氏距离，并基于 Fejes--Tóth 最小弦距离界推导理论上界。提出 S-Opt：利用球面 packing 解构造星座；提出 Z-Opt：基于 Bloch 球上堆叠正多边形构造星座。同时设计 S-Opt 与 Z-Opt 两种低复杂度检测器。

Result: S-Opt 在所考虑的最优 Bloch 球 packing 情形下达到推导的上界；S-Opt 检测器适用于任意 \mathcal{G}(2,1) Grassmannian 星座，复杂度随接收天线数线性增长、随星座大小对数增长，且性能与 GLRT 相同。Z-Opt 的最小弦距离在评估星座规模下接近上界；Z-Opt 检测器复杂度随接收天线数线性增长，并在 Z-Opt 星座上达到与 GLRT 相同的检测性能。

Conclusion: 通过 Bloch 球表示，论文将 Grassmannian 星座构造与检测转化为更直观且高效的球面几何问题。S-Opt 更偏向最优 packing 性能，Z-Opt 更具结构化与检测复杂度优势，二者均为 \mathcal{G}(2,1) 非相干通信提供了高性能、低复杂度方案。

Abstract: Grassmannian constellations are known to achieve the capacity of noncoherent communications over Rayleigh fading channels in the high-SNR regime, yet their efficient construction remains challenging. In this paper, we propose two construction methods for Grassmannian constellations of one-dimensional subspaces in a two-dimensional space, termed S-Opt and Z-Opt, along with two low-complexity detectors. Both the construction and detection procedures are performed on the unit sphere, known as the Bloch sphere in quantum computing. We show that the chordal distance on the Grassmann manifold is proportional to the Euclidean distance on the Bloch sphere and derive a corresponding theoretical upper bound based on the Fejes--Tóth bound on the minimum chordal distance. The S-Opt constellation is constructed from sphere-packing solutions and attains the derived upper bound for the optimal Bloch-sphere packings considered. The S-Opt detector can be applied to arbitrary Grassmannian constellations on $\mathcal{G}(2,1)$, and its time complexity scales linearly with the number of receive antennas and logarithmically with the constellation size, while yielding the same detection performance as the GLRT detector. Furthermore, based on the insight obtained through the S-Opt construction, the Z-Opt constellation is constructed by stacking regular polygons on the Bloch sphere, and its minimum chordal distance approaches the derived upper bound over the evaluated constellation sizes. The Z-Opt detector's time complexity scales linearly with the number of receive antennas, while yielding the same detection performance as the GLRT detector for Z-Opt.

</details>

Method: 作者采用级联码构造LRC：以内码保证局部修复结构，以定义在F4上的线性码作为外码；提出系统化的外码选择策略，使所得二元LRC具备最优参数。所得码的重量分布由所选F4线性码的重量分布决定。

Abstract: In recent years, locally repairable codes (LRCs) have attracted considerable attention owing to their pivotal role in distributed storage systems. Since binary linear locally repairable codes can significantly reduce the complexity of both encoding and decoding processes, the construction of binary LRCs has attracted extensive research interest. In this paper, we construct locally repairable codes via concatenated codes and present a systematic approach to select outer codes to obtain optimal binary LRCs, where the outer codes are linear codes over $\mathbb{F}_4$. The weight distributions of the resulting LRCs are determined by the weight distributions of the selected linear codes over $\mathbb{F}_4$. Furthermore, several classes of optimal binary locally repairable codes are constructed, including binary LRCs meeting the Griesmer-like bound, and binary perfect LRCs. Meanwhile, for the locality $r=2$, we improve the Johnson-like bound for binary LRCs with disjoint local repair groups established by Ma and Ge, and construct explicit LRCs that attain this new bound.

### [149] [A Framework of Secure Source Coding using Mutual Information Security Criterion: Universal Coding, Strong Converse Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04720)
*Yasutada Oohama,Bagus Santoso*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出一种固定长度源编码上的源加密框架，给出可靠与安全通信的充要条件，并证明该条件具有强逆定理且存在分布无关的通用加解密方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统安全通信常以 Shannon 密码系统为基础，但针对先进行固定长度源编码再加密的“源加密”场景，需要明确在允许一定解码错误率与信息泄漏上界时，可靠性和安全性可同时达成的精确条件。

Method: 作者构建源加密框架，将密码处理施加于规定长度的源代码；以互信息度量对手获得的信息泄漏；在错误概率不超过 ε、信息泄漏不超过 δ 的约束下，推导可靠安全通信的必要且充分条件，并进一步分析该条件对 ε 与 δ 的依赖性。

Result: 论文显式建立了可靠且安全通信的充要条件；证明该条件不依赖于任意 ε∈(0,1) 与 δ∈(0,∞)，从而得到该框架下的强逆定理；同时证明存在对明文分布和密钥分布均通用有效的加密/解密方案。

Conclusion: 该工作为固定长度源编码场景下的源加密提供了信息论层面的精确可达性刻画，表明安全可靠通信存在清晰阈值，并且可通过通用方案实现，具有较强的理论完备性。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a framework of source encryption, where cryptographic processing is applied to a prescribed fixed length source code. The proposed source encryption framework is based on the secure communication framework of the Shannon cipher system. In the proposed framework, we use the mutual information as a measure of information leakage to an adversary. For the proposed framework, we explicitly establish the necessary and sufficient condition for reliable and secure communication under the condition that error probability and information leakage, respectively, are upper bounded by prescribed constants $ε\in (0,1)$ and $δ\in (0,\infty)$. We also show that the obtained necessary and sufficient condition does not depend on the constants $ε\in (0,1)$ and $δ\in (0,\infty)$, demonstrating that we have the strong converse theorem for the proposed framework of source encryption. We further prove the existence of encryption/decryption schemes, which are universal in the sense that they work effectively for any distributions of the plain text and those of the key used for the encryption.

</details>


### [150] [Phased Ultra Massive Array (PUMA)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04866)
*Hanjiang Hong,Kai-Kit Wong,Xusheng Zhu,Chenguang Rao,Dazhi He,Hyundong Shin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出PUMA多址框架，将用户端流体天线系统的空间灵活性与相控阵模拟合并结合，在少量甚至单RF链条件下实现高增益与干扰抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面向6G海量连接场景，传统多址和大规模天线方案往往依赖基站端CSI预编码或用户端复杂干扰消除，硬件复杂度和RF链数量较高；因此需要一种在用户设备侧具备低复杂度、高硬件效率、且对共用户干扰不敏感的接入架构。

Method: 在FAMA与CUMA基础上提出phased ultra massive antenna array（PUMA）。该架构在UE侧利用FAS提供的空间位置可调性，并引入相控阵进行模拟域相移与信号聚合，从而在空间域内自然缓解共用户干扰；同时对可达数据率进行理论分析，并通过仿真评估性能。

Result: 理论与仿真结果表明，PUMA在可达速率方面显著优于FAMA和CUMA，尤其是在UE仅配置单个RF链时优势明显；其能够在低RF链数量下获得较高天线增益并提升干扰鲁棒性。

Conclusion: PUMA是一种面向6G海量连接的高效多址方案，通过UE侧空间灵活性和模拟域相控合并，在无需BS端CSI预编码或复杂UE端干扰消除的情况下，实现可扩展、低硬件复杂度和干扰不敏感的通信。

Abstract: This paper proposes a novel multiple-access framework, termed the phased ultra massive antenna array (PUMA), which exploits the distinctive spatial flexibility of fluid antenna systems (FAS) at the user equipment (UE). Building upon fluid antenna multiple access (FAMA) and compact ultra-massive antenna array (CUMA), PUMA incorporates a phased array for signal aggregation. This architecture enables the UE to inherently mitigate co-user interference within the spatial domain without necessitating channel state information (CSI) for precoding at the base station (BS) or complex interference cancellation at each UE. A primary advantage of PUMA lies in its hardware efficiency: by implementing phase shifting and signal combining in the analog domain, it achieves high antenna gain while requiring only a minimal number of radio-frequency (RF) chains, potentially a single RF chain. Comprehensive theoretical analysis of the achievable data rate is provided, complemented by extensive simulations that validate the framework. The results demonstrate that PUMA markedly outperforms FAMA and CUMA architectures, particularly for UEs with a single RF chain, offering a robust and scalable solution for interference-insensitive massive connectivity in sixth-generation (6G) systems.

</details>


### [151] [Deterministic identification for Bernoulli channels and related channels with continuous input](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05168)
*Pau Colomer,Christian Deppe,Holger Boche,Andreas Winter*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文将“galaxy”码优化构造从 AWGN 信道推广到 Bernoulli 信道及一类输出分布像包含连续曲线的信道，证明其确定性识别容量常数为 1/2，并改进小误差指数区域的可靠性下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续输入字母表的无记忆信道中，确定性识别（DI）的消息规模通常呈 n log n 量级增长，但长期存在可达界与反 converse 界之间的缺口；同时 DI 的速率—可靠性折中也存在类似缺口。

Method: 基于近期用于 AWGN 信道的优化 galaxy 码构造，先针对 Bernoulli 信道建立代码与分析，再利用任意信道 W 的输出分布像若包含连续曲线，则可在输入子区间上约化为 Bernoulli 信道的思想进行推广；同时分析该码的速率与错误概率指数关系。

Result: 证明对该广泛信道类，已有 converse bound 是紧的，并得到确定性识别容量 dot{C}_{DI}(W)=1/2；在可靠性函数方面给出改进的下界，且在小误差指数区域的一阶主导项上逼近 converse。

Conclusion: 论文关闭了连续输入无记忆信道 DI 容量中的长期缺口，并表明优化 galaxy 码及 Bernoulli 约化技术可作为处理更一般信道 DI 问题的有效工具。

Abstract: For memoryless channels with continuous input alphabets, deterministic identification (DI) typically exhibits a linearithmic ($n\log n$) message growth. However, the exact DI capacity has long remained open due to a persistent gap between the best known achievability and converse bounds. This gap was recently closed for AWGN channels via a novel code construction optimising the "galaxy" codes. Here, we extend this approach to the Bernoulli channel and subsequently to any channel $W$ whose image contains a continuous curve of output probability distributions, and hence admits a reduction to the Bernoulli channel restricted to a subinterval of inputs. As a consequence, we prove that the converse bound is tight and establish $\dot{C}_{\text{DI}}(W) = \frac 12$ for this broad class of channels, thereby closing the long-standing capacity gap. A similar gap was also observed for the DI rate-reliability tradeoff. We analyse the tradeoff between rate and error of the proposed code and derive improved lower bounds on the reliability function, approaching the converse at leading order in the regime of small error exponents.

</details>


### [152] [Private Contiguous-Block Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05169)
*Maha Issa,Anoosheh Heidarzadeh*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出并研究私有连续块检索（PCBR）问题：用户从分布在多个非串通服务器上的有序消息中私密检索连续的 D 个消息。论文给出了平衡 {0,1}-线性方案的速率上界、达到该上界所需的子分组下界，并构造了在较广参数范围内速率最优且子分组最优的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存储与流媒体系统中，文件常被切分为有序片段，用户通常请求连续片段块而非任意消息子集。传统多消息私有信息检索（MPIR）允许请求任意 D 个消息，未利用“连续性”结构。论文旨在回答：限制请求为连续块是否能提升检索效率或降低方案复杂度。

Method: 作者形式化定义 PCBR 问题，并聚焦于平衡 {0,1}-线性检索方案。论文推导了所有参数下可达检索速率的上界；进一步证明若要达到该速率上界，方案必须满足的子分组级别下界；随后构造一种利用连续块结构的检索方案，并分析其速率与子分组复杂度。

Result: 论文证明 PCBR 的最优速率与已有 MPIR 速率 converse bound 相一致；但现有 MPIR 方案直接用于 PCBR 时可能并非最优，且往往需要更高子分组。作者构造的 PCBR 专用方案在较广参数范围内达到速率上界，同时其子分组水平匹配理论下界。

Conclusion: PCBR 作为 MPIR 的结构化特例，可以利用请求块的连续性降低实现复杂度。尽管速率上不一定超过已知 MPIR 上界，连续块结构可显著改善子分组需求，并使方案更适合有序分段存储和流式访问场景。

Abstract: We introduce the \emph{Private Contiguous-Block Retrieval (PCBR)} problem, where a user retrieves a block of $D$ messages with contiguous indices from $K$ replicated messages stored across $N$ non-colluding servers, while hiding the identity of the requested block from each server. This problem is motivated by storage and streaming systems where files are split into ordered segments. Unlike multi-message Private Information Retrieval (MPIR), where any $D$-subset may be requested, PCBR restricts the demand family to contiguous blocks. This relaxation raises a natural question: Can this structure be exploited to improve retrieval efficiency? We answer this question for balanced $\{0,1\}$-linear schemes. We establish an upper bound on the achievable retrieval rate for all problem parameters, derive a lower bound on the subpacketization level required by any scheme achieving the rate upper bound, and construct a rate-optimal scheme whose subpacketization level matches the lower bound for a broad range of problem parameters. Although the optimal PCBR rate coincides with the best-known MPIR rate converse bound, existing MPIR schemes can be suboptimal for PCBR and can require a much larger subpacketization level. In contrast, our scheme exploits the contiguous-block structure to achieve the optimal rate with reduced subpacketization.

</details>


### [153] [Optimizing Bit-Labeling of Voronoi Constellations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05202)
*Carilyn Rumrill,David Muzzey,Connor Davis,Stephen Mackes,Dan Chew*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出一种用于优化 D4 与 E8 根格比特到符号映射的搜索方法与性能度量，在固定格星座的条件下通过搜索基矩阵置换整数标签，获得 BER 性能增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在格调制中，格点的比特标记方式会影响比特错误率。既有文献常用标准基，但这些基未必对应最优的 bit-to-symbol 映射。作者希望在不改变格星座、从而控制其他格增益来源的情况下，仅优化标签映射以提升 BER。

Method: 固定 D4 和 E8 根格的格星座，考虑能够置换格点整数标签的不同基矩阵；定义新的搜索方法和性能指标，用于评估不同基矩阵对应的比特到符号映射，并在候选基矩阵空间中进行搜索。

Result: 相较于文献中常用的标准基，在 BER = 10^-4 时，优化后的 D4 映射获得约 0.1 dB 的 BER 曲线增益，E8 映射获得约 0.5 dB 的增益。

Conclusion: 比特到符号映射本身是影响格调制 BER 的重要因素；即使固定格星座，仅通过选择更合适的基矩阵/标签置换，也能为 D4 和尤其是 E8 根格带来可观的误码率性能提升。

Abstract: We define a novel search method and performance metric as a technique for optimizing the bit-to-symbol map of the $D_4$ and $E_8$ root lattices in reference to bit error rate. We hold other sources of lattice gain constant by fixing the lattice constellation, and consider basis matrices that permute the integer labelings of the lattice points. After searching the possible basis matrices for $D_4$ and $E_8$, we found 0.1 dB of gain in $D_4$ bit error rate curves, and 0.5 dB of gain in $E_8$ compared to the standard bases commonly used in literature at a BER of $10^{-4}$.

</details>
